## How to view mail in the iPostal1 App inbox

You can view all of your mail items and manage your mail conveniently on your mobile device. Please download the iPostal1 App from your devices Apple App store or Google Play store. To view your mail in the iPostal1 App: Step 1. Log on to your account in the iPostal1 App, using your username and password. Step 2. Scroll through your mail items in your Inbox to view the image of each mail item and the date the item was received. Step 3. Tap on the item for more details or tap on the green icon to make a request for that item.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## How to view Service and Pricing Options in the iPostal1 App

You can view prices for additional services before making a request for your mail items directly in the iPostal1 App. To view prices in the iPostal1 App: Step 1. Log into your account in the iPostal1 App, using your username and password. Step 2. Tap on the Menu icon, located on the top left corner. Step 3. You will see a menu of options, tap on " Pricing" to view prices for optional services. Step 4. Here you can view all available services and pricing options for your mail items.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## How to find the Task Toolbar Menu in the iPostal1 App

The Task Toolbar is located in your account when logged in to the App. Here you will find the options that enables you to make requests for your mail items such as: Ship, Scan, Consolidate, Schedule Pick Up, Cancel Requests, and Discard. To access your Task Toolb ar: Step 1. Log into your account in the iPostal1 App, using your username and password. Step 2. Tap on the green icon on the left of your selected mail item. Or tap on the Mail Item and tap on the Task Toolbar in the upper right corner. Step 3. Here you will view all of the options available for your mail items. Note: To return mail items to sender, please contact your mail center directly.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## How to View a Scanned Document in the iPostal1 App

Once your scan request is processed by your mail center, you will be able to view the scanned documents in your accounts inbox. To view the scan in the App: Step 1. Log into your account in the iPostal1 App, using your username and password. Step 2. Tap on your Scanned Mail item. Step 3. Tap on the Scanned image to view. You can download and save the images to your device.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## How to Add Folders in the iPostal1 App

Adding folders to your Inbox is a great way to keep your mail items organized. You can simply create personalized folders for your mail items directly from the App. To Add folders in the iPostal1 Mobile App: Step 1. Log into your account in the iPostal1 App, using your username and password. Step 2. Tap on the drop down arrow located in the center top toolbar, next to "Inbox" . Step 3. Tap on " + Add Folders" . Step 4. Enter the name of your new folder and tap on " Add" , located at the bottom right. Step 5. Tap on the " Inbox" dropdown to view your new folder. You can now move any mail items into this folders by clicking on the mail item from your inbox, click on the "Menu" icon at the top right, click on "Move to".

## I received an alert that I have new mail but I cannot see it?

If you cannot view new mail in your inbox and are experiencing technical difficulties with the app, p lease ensure your app is updated to the latest version. If no updates are available, we recommend uninstalling and reinstalling the app, as this often resolves common technical issues.

## How to ship mail using the iPostal1 App

Shipping your mail is simple via the iPostal1 App. To begin, login to the iPostal1 App using your username and password. Shipping one single mail item: you can select the mail item, and click on "Ship" . Shipping more than one i tem: you will need to consolidate the mail first, in order for shipping options to show. Shipping multiple mail items together in one st ep: choose a " Consolidate and Ship " instead. Note: The shipping address that is entered must be valid USPS address. International shipping may vary by country and by mail center location. How to create a shipping request in the iPostal1 App: Step 1. Log into your account in the iPostal1 App, using your username and password. Select the mail item that you wish to ship by tapping on the green icon to left of your mail item number. A menu will appear immediately on the right side of your screen. Then tap " Ship" . or you can also click on the image of the mail item to view the menu icon, at the top right. Step 2. Select the address where you wish to ship the mail item(s) and and tap "Next" . Step 3. Enter any special Instructions and/or signature option and tap " Next". Step 4. Choose your preferred shipping method and tap " Next". Step 5. Verify that your information is accurate and tap " Send Request" to complete your order. Your mail center will automatically receive your request and will ship your mail soon. The status in your Inbox will be updated to " Ship Requested" . After your request has been processed, the item will be removed from your inbox. You can confirm that the request was completed by checking your m ail history . Note: All shipping labels are generated at your mail center, prepaid, p rivate or personal labels are not allowed for shipping.

## How to scan mail items in the iPostal1 App

You can request a scan of the inside contents of your mail items and view the images, conveniently from the iPostal1 App. Credit Cards and Gift Cards cannot be scanned. To scan a mail item in your iPostal1 App: Step 1. Log into your account in the iPostal1 App, using your username and password. Step 2 . Select the Items of mail that you wish to scan by tapping on the green icon, located to the left of the mail item number. Then tap " Scan" in the Inbox Menu. or you can tap on the mail item itself and then tap on the taskbar menu, located in the top right corner. Step 3. Select a scan option and tap " Send Request" , located at the bottom right corner. Step 4. The status of your mail item will now read " Scan Requested" . After your mail center has processed your order, the status will be updated to " Scanned" . After your mail center has processed your order, the status will be updated to " Scanned" . To View the scanned item, tap on the mail item in your inbox and then tap on the image.

## How to consolidate to get a shipping quote in the iPostal1 App

You can choose to consolidate several mail items at once. After your consolidate request has been processed, your mail items will be combined into one package and you will then be able to view a shipping quote. For consolidation task status or changes please contact your mail center directly. To consolidate your mail items in the iPostal1 App: Step 1. Log into your account in the iPostal1 App, using your username and password. Step 2 . Select the items of mail that you wish to consolidate by tapping on the green icon to the left of the shipping number. Then tap on " Consolidate" in the Inbox Menu. Step 3. Confirm your order by tapping " Se nd Request". Step 4. The status for the mail items will change to " Consolidate Requested". After your mail center has processed your order, the status will be updated to " Consolidated" . After your mail center process the consolidation request, usually within 24-48hrs, your consolidated mail items will appear together in one new package. The mail item number will begin with the letter "C". Once your new consolidated mail item appears in your inbox, select the mail item starting with a "C" to begin a shipping task. You will then see real-time shipping rates when creating a shipping task for that mail item. Storage fees are applicable for each individual mail item, until the mail items are shipped. The buttons to ship will not be accessible/gray, until the request is fully processed by you mail center.

## How to Schedule a Pick Up in the iPostal1 App

Before picking up mail at your mail center address, we recommend you schedule a pickup. You can pickup mail during business hours listed at your location. Once your pickup is scheduled, y our mail center will receive an alert that you are coming in to pick up your mail. When you arrive to pick up mail: You will be asked for ID. You will be asked to sign for your mail items. You may be charged a small fee when you pickup the mail at your mail center. To schedule a pickup in the iPostal1 App: Step 1. Log into your account in the iPostal1 App, using your username and password. Step 2. Select the Items(s) of mail you would like to pick up by tapping on the green icons to the left of the mail item number. Then tap " Schedule Pick Up" in the Inbox Menu. Step 3. Choose an available date and time. Step 4. Tap Send request to complete your order.

Select the Items(s) of mail that you wish to discard and then tap on the green icon on the left side of your screen. Step 3. Tap " Discard". or you can tap on the mail item itself and then tap on the taskbar menu in the top right corner. Your mail center will receive the notification and the mail item(s) will be removed from your inbox within 24-48hrs.

## How to request an image of box contents in the iPostal1 App

If you would like to view the images of the inside contents of a package, you can choose a box image request for your mail. Your mail center will open your package and take pictures of the inside of your package. The cost of this service is $3.95. To request a picture of the insides of your package in the iPostal1 App: Step 1. Log into your account in the iPostal1 App, using your username and email. Step 2. Select the designated package and press the green icon on left side of your screen. Step 3. Tap " Box Images" . or you can tap on the mail item itself and then tap on the taskbar menu, located in the top right corner. Step 4. Select one: " Box Images" only, " Invoice" images only, or both "I mages and Invoices". Tap " Send Request". Your mail center will receive an alert to process your request. Once the request is completed, you will be able to view the images from inside of your iPostal1 App.

## How to Shred Mail Items in the iPostal1 App

We recommend selecting a shred for any important mail items. Requesting a shred is simple in the iPostal1 App. The price to shred mail items is $2.25 per letter and includes up to 10 pages. Discounted Scan/Shred Bundles are available for purchase inside your inbox. To shred a mail item in the iPostal1 Mobile App: Step 1. Log into your account in the iPostal1 App, using your username and password. Step 2. Select the mail item(s) that you wish to shred and then tap on the green icon on the left side of the mail item. Step 3. Tap " Shred" . or tap on the mail item itself and then tap on the taskbar menu, located in the top right corner. Your mail center will receive an alert to process your request. The status below your mail item will be updated to " Shred Requested" . You will receive an email confirmation when your mail has been shredded and t he mail item will be removed from your inbox.

## How to Add Another Location Address to your Account in the iPostal1 App

You can add a new iPostal1 address to receive mail conveniently from your mobile device. Simply choose your plan and your account will automatically be charged for the new monthly subscription. For locations in the U.S., a new notarized form 1583 and 2 acceptable IDs must be submitted for each individual address you sign up for. For locations outside of the U.S., Please contact customer support as the requirements may be different. To add another Virtual Mailbox account in the App: Step 1. Log into your account in the iPostal1 App, using your username and password. Step 2. Tap on the " Menu" icon, located in the top left corner. Step 3. Tap on " Add Location" . Step 4. Choose a State and choose a City. Step 5 . Select the designated store address you wish to add. Step 6. Select the type of mailbox and plan you wish to subscribe to and tap "Confirm" to create the new mailbox address for your account.

## How to Enable Auto-Scan in the iPostal1 App

The Auto-Scan feature will automatically scan all mail items inside of your inbox upon arrival. T he charge for scanning the inside contents of mail will apply when this feature is enabled. Note : Please see our Scanning Prices and Bundles to learn more about prices. To turn on Auto-Scan on the iPostal1 App: Step 1. Log on to your iPostal1 App using your username and password. Step 2. Tap on the " Menu" icon, located in the top left corner. Step 3. Tap on " Account Settings" . Step 4. Tap on " M ailbox Configuration". Step 5. Tap on the Auto-Scan Documents to toggle On . Step 6 . Tap " Done" at the bottom right.

## How to set up Automatic Shipping in the iPostal1 App

The Auto ship feature will automatically ship any mail you receive based on frequency you select. You are charged per shipment, based on the mail item dimensions, the carrier and speed you choose and the shipping rates set at your mail center location. To set up automatic shipping in the iPostal1 App: Step 1. Log on to your iPostal1 App using your username and password. Step 2. Tap on the " Menu" icon, located in the top left corner. Step 3. Tap on " Account Settings" . Step 4. Tap on " Mailbox Configuration" . Step 5. Select your shipping frequency based on the options provided: upon request, weekly, every two weeks or monthly. If you select "Upon Request", autoship will not be activated. You will be required to login each time you would like to create a shipment. Step 6. Choose your preferred "Domestic Shipping Level" . Step 7. Tap "Done" . *You can log back into your account to change your shipping settings at any time.

## How to cancel my account in the iPostal1 App

You can choose to cancel your account at any time in the iPostal1 app. Before canceling your account, please be sure to empty the contents of your mailbox by selecting an action for your mail such as, discard, pick up, shred or ship and be sure that your payment is up to date. Once your account is cleared of its contents and up to date, you can proceed to close your account. To cancel your account in the iPostal1 App: Step 1. Log into your account in the iPostal1 App, using your username or password. Step 2. Tap on the " Menu" button in the top left corner. Be sure that all mail is cleared from your inbox. Step 3. Tap on " Account Settings", below your mailbox address. Step 4. Tap "Cancel Mailbox " . Step 5. The system will ask you to confirm that this is what you would like to do. If you cancel your account by mistake, please contact customer. Once you cancel your mailbox, your account will be closed completely , mail will no longer be accepted at your location. Please remember to update your contacts with your new mailing address. If the Cancel Mailbox link is not clickable, please take action on the mail items in your account and be sure your payment is up to date.

## How to Schedule a Pick Up

You or any additional recipient on your account can pick up your mail in person at your mail center address by requesting a Schedule Pick Up from inside your inbox. Scheduling a pick-up will ensure that your mail will be updated when you arrive which prevents unnecessary storage charges. Your mail center will ask for ID when picking up mail and a small fee may be charged to pick up. If you need someone else to pick up your mail, they must be added to the account and submit the required documents. You can find your locations pick up hours directly in mailbox. If you may have any questions on pick up hours, please contact your mail center directly. Your mail center location address is located in your account at the top left. If the pick up option is greyed and you are unable to click this option, please click on the mail items you are picking up first. Verify that your payment is up to date, if your payment is not up to date, you will not be able to schedule a pick up. To Schedule a Pick Up: Step 1. Login to your account on a desktop or mobile browser. Select the mail item(s) from inside your inbox and click on the "Schedule Pickup" button from the Top Toolbar. Step 2. Select an available pickup date by clicking on the calendar date, then you can proceed to choose a time for your scheduled pick-up. Step 3. To finish, scroll down and click the "Schedule" button to complete your request. Note: Your mail center will receive an alert that you are coming in to pick up your mail on the date and time selected. When you arrive, you will be asked for ID, you will sign for your mail items and you will be charged the pickup fee. Personal Delivery is also offered in some areas at an additional cost.

## How to request a shipment for a single mail item?

Creating a shipping request can easily send or forward your mail to your home address or another valid address. After you have submitted your shipping request, y our mail center will receive an alert to process. Once the request is completed, you will receive an email confirmation with the order details and tracking number, if you selected a trackable shipping method. Your shipping address must be a valid USPS address. International shipping varies by country and by location. How to create a shipping request in your account: Step 1. Login to your account on a desktop or mobile browser. Select the item you would like to ship and click on the " Ship " button on the top toolbar. The "Ship" option is only available for one item. If you are shipping multiple items, you can choose "Consolidate & Ship" , and all of the mail will become one item with new a weight and dimensions. Please allow 24 - 48 hrs for all request to be processed. For shipping request status, please contact your mail center directly. If you are shipping packages internationally, please ensure that you have completed the online notary session during sign up. If you receive an error or may need assistance with completing an online notary, after the initial sign up process, please contact customer support. Please ensure that all shipping addresses that are entered, are valid, verified and recognized by USPS to avoid any delivery issues. If you shipped a mail item and selected an incorrect address address, please contact your mail center immediately. Step 2. Select a valid USPS Shipping Address where you would like to have your mail to shipped to. If the address is displayed in the center dropdown, Click the " Continue" button located at the bottom right of the page. Y ou can add a new address by clicking on " +Add a New Address " . Fill in the required information and click on " Add Shipping Address" when finished. Step 3. Fill in the required information and enter any special instructions at the bottom of the page (if applicable) and click " Continue " when finished. Step 4. S elect your shipping method. The mail will be sent out with the carrier of your choice. Click " Continue" when finished. Step 5. Verify that all your information is correct, and c lick " Ship" when finished. Note: All shipping labels are generated at your mail center, prepaid, p rivate or personal labels are not allowed for shipping.

## How to ship multiple mail items at once?

Save time and request a "Consolidate and Ship" for all of your mail items at once. Your mail center will combine the selected mail items together and ship according to your selected options. When you choose this option, you will not see any shipping rates or prices. When consolidating and shipping in one step, a price quote is not provided. If you would like to view a price for shipping, please request a "Consolidation" first. If you are shipping internationally, please ensure that you have completed the online notary session. Note: All shipping labels are generated at your mail center, prepaid, p rivate or personal labels are not allowed for shipping. When adding a shipping address, please ensure that all shipping addresses that are entered, are valid, verified and recognized by USPS to avoid any delivery issues. To ship multiple mail items at once: Step 1. Login to your account on a desktop or mobile browser. Select all of the mail items you would like to ship together, and choose the " Consolidate & Ship" button on the top toolbar. Step 2. Select a shipping address from the drop down menu. You can also click the "Add a New address" button, if needed. Step 3. Select Optional Services or enter Special Instructions, if needed. Step 4. Choose your shipping method and click the " Continue" button. The mail item will be shipped with the carrier that you select. The price will depend on the carrier, the shipping speed, the weight and dimensions of the combined letters or package. Step 5. Please verify that all your information is correct and click the " Ship" button. Step 6. Your Mail Center will get an alert to process your request click " OK" to close the window. Please allow 24 - 48 hrs for your request to be processed by your mail center. You will receive an email confirmation when your mail has been shipped. A tracking number will be included in your confirmation order, only if you have chosen a trackable shipping method. If you would like a quote in advance of shipping, please choose a "Consolidation" of mail more. If the "Ship" option is not active or gray, please ensure you click on the mail items first or check if the mail item is already involved in another pending request. If you owe a balance you will not be able to proceed until your payment is updated.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## How to get a shipping quote for multiple mail items or packages?

To receive a shipping quote for shipping multiple mail items together, you can request a consolidation of mail. Your mail center location will combine all the selected mail items into one package. You will receive an alert when it is completed, so you can log in and choose your desired shipping option with the correct pricing. If you are shipping packages internationally, please ensure that you have notarized your documents using the online notary. Storage fees will continue to be charged for each individual mail item, until the mail items are shipped. How to Consolidate multiple mail items: Step 1. Login to your account on a desktop or mobile browser. S elect two or more mail items, then click on the Consolidate Button in the top toolbar . Step 2. Enter special instructions for your mail center in the text box. Then c lick the " Consolidate" b utton . The cost for consolidation is $1.95 per package, letters and postcards are free to consolidate. Step 3. To finish, Click " Ok" to submit your request. Your mail center will receive an alert to process your request and send you an email confirmation when completed. Note: The new consolidated mail item ID will begin with the letter "C". After your consolidation is complete , you can log into your account and request a shipment for your consolidated mail item. You will then see a quoted price for shipping.

## How to discard mail I don't want?

We understand that you may receive items in your inbox that you don't need. You can choose to discard mail items free of charge. Your mail center will dispose of the unwanted mail items you include in your request and the mail item will be deleted from your inbox. If your mail items are important, we recommend you choose the mail Shredding option instead. Step 1. Login to your account on a desktop or mobile browser. S elect the mail item(s) you wish to discard from your inbox. Then, click on the "Discard" button in the top toolbar. Step 2. Click Continue to submit your request. Step 3. To finish, click " Ok" to complete the process. Your Mail Center will get an alert to process your request and you will receive an email confirmation when it is completed. For discard request status, please contact your mail center directly. Note: Discarding mail is a request to take the mail and place it in the regular trash or recycling. Once mail is discarded the image is deleted from our system. If you have requested a discard in error and the task is still pending, you can cancel the request. If the task was already processed, please contact your mail center directly for assistance.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## How to request a scan of the inside contents of your mail item?

You can request a scan to view the inside contents of your letter. When selecting to scan, your mail center will open the envelope and scan the images. After the task is completed, the images will be in your inbox for you to view. The charge for a scan of the inside contents is $2.25 for the first 10 pages of each letter and $.25 each additional page. Scan/Shred bundles are available for purchase at a discount in the top right corner of your screen. Credit Cards and Gift Cards cannot be scanned. Step 1. Login to your account on a desktop or mobile browser. Select the mail item that you would like to be scanned and click on the "Scan" button in the toolbar above. Step 2. Choose an option for what you want to do with the mail after the scan has been completed. Scan and Put Back in My Mailbox : Original mail will be saved until you choose to Ship, Pickup, Shred or Discard. Scan and Discard : Scan will be saved in your inbox, and original mail will be discarded. Scan and Shred : Scan will be saved in your inbox, and original mail will be shredded. Please note that shredding cannot be reversed once it is completed and a small fee is added for the shredding request. Step 3. Scroll down and click on " Scan" to submit your request. The status of your mail item will be updated to " Scan Requested" in your inbox immediately after you submit your request. Processing time: If you have already requested a Scan, please allow 24 - 48hrs or 1-2 business days for your mail center to process. If you need an update on the status of your request, please contact your mail center directly. When your order has been fulfilled, the status will read " Scanned" . Viewing your scan: Your completed scan will be viewable as a PDF in your inbox. You can download your PDF and email it as an attachment. Save any scans: The scanned images are deleted from our system once you select an action, such as: discard, ship, pick up, shred etc. You will no longer be able to view these in your inbox. Please be sure to save the images of your scan. Issue with your scan: If your scanned images are not visible, missing a page, incorrect or you have an issue with the quality of the scan, please contact customer support for assistance.

## How to shred mail items

You can choose to shred a mail item and your mail center will open the letter and shred the inside contents of the letter. The fee to shred is $2.25 per letter. This includes up to 10 pages and $.25 for each additional page. Discounted Scan/Shred Bundles can be purchased by clicking on the underlined link above your top toolbar. Step 1. Login to your account on a desktop or mobile browser. S elect the mail item you wish to shred from your inbox and then click the " Shred" button located in the t op toolbar . Step 2. Click " Continue". Step 3. To finish, Click on " Ok" to submit your request. Your Mail Center will receive an alert to process your request, and you will receive an email confirmation when it is completed. Please allow 24 - 48 hrs for all tasks to be processed. Note: Once mail is shredded, it is no longer available to view. To check the status of your Shred request please contact your mail center. If you need to cancel a shredding request, please contact your mail center immediately.

## How to Deposit a Check

You can choose to deposit a check to conveniently from your iPostal1 Mailbox directly to your bank account. Checks are shipped to your bank via USPS and will include a tracking number. Each check that you would like deposited will need to be scanned, before you can proceed to request a check deposit task. Note: The cost for each check deposit request is $4.95, plus the cost of trackable USPS Shipping (on average $11-15) You may deposit up to 5 checks per check deposit request. This service is limited to Mail Centers in the United States. If the check has not been scanned, the option to scan will not be available to choose. Step 1. Before you can request a check deposit, please request a "Scan" of the check first . After the check is scanned by your mail center, you will be able to proceed. Click on the scanned check that you would like to deposit. Click on " C heck Deposit" button from the top toolbar. Step 2. Select your bank account information. You can add your bank account information in your "Account Settings", located at the top toolbar by clicking the drop down next to your username. Step 3. Choose your preferred shipping method. All Checks will be mailed via a USPS trackable service. You can expect to be charged a shipping fee plus a charge for check processing. Step 4. Enter the required check details below including: Bank name on check Account number on check Amount of check Check date Step 5. Click on the " Deposit Button" to complete your order. A tracking number will be generated and accessible in the transaction section of your account, once your mail center has processed the request. To check the status of your Check Deposit request, please contact your mail center directly.

Personal Delivery allows you to schedule the delivery of your mail items directly to your home. You can pick a date and time that works for you and a driver will deliver your mail. Note: This option is available for letters, large envelopes, letter packs and packages under 50lb. Personal deliveries can be scheduled up to 3 days in advance in 3 hour time slots. The cost varies based on the time of day that you are requesting the delivery. The quote is only valid for 15 minutes as traffic and demand fluctuate. To schedule a Personal Delivery: 1. Login to your account on a desktop or mobile browser. S elect the mail items to be delivered, c lick on "Personal Delivery" . 2. Confirm your delivery address. 3. Select your preferred date and time, click: " Continue" . 4 . Enter the value of your mail items, confirm your contact information, select a signature option, add an optional tip and add special instructions. 5 . Review the details, click the terms of service checkbox, and click "Submit Order" .

Note: You will be required to empty your Inbox by discarding, shredding, shipping, or picking up any remaining mail items before transferring to a new location. ## How to Enable Automatic Shipping

The Autoship feature allows you to set the frequency with which all your mail items are automatically shipped to your shipping address on record. Once a mail item is received at your mail center, it will be shipped according to your selection. Each shipment will be charged based on the shipping rates at your location. The shipping address that is entered must be valid USPS address. International shipping may vary by country and by mail center location. To enable the Autoship feature: Step 1. Login to your account on a desktop or mobile browser. Click on " Mailbox Settings" located in the left toolbar. Note: The default setting is "No Autoship" . Step 2. Choose an Autoship frequency by clicking on the dropdown menu located under "Autoship Options" and make your selection (Weekly/Every Two Weeks/Monthly). Step 3. Click on " Ok". Step 4. Scroll down to the " Autoship Options" box and click on the dropdown menus below to select your desired International/Domestic Carrier settings. Note : You will need to make a selection for both International and Domestic, even if you are only shipping domestic. Step 5. P lease select the day of the week you would like your items shipped and whether or not you would like to be notified each time a shipment is prepared. Note: Please ensure that all shipping addresses that are entered, are valid, verified and recognized by USPS to avoid any delivery issues.

## Can I pause my iPostal1 Subscription?

The " O n Hold" feature allows approved accounts to place their mailbox on hold for a duration of three, six, or twelve months for a one-time fee. This feature applies to customers who have been active for three or more months and have yet to come off a hold within the last three months. You will retain the mailbox number and address throughout the hold period without needing to notarize a new Form 1583 to reopen the account. Note: Please be sure to empty your Inbox by discarding, shipping, or scheduling a Pick Up for your mail items, and pay any outstanding balance; otherwise, the hold feature will not be available. To place an account On Hold: Step 1. Log in to your account on a desktop or mobile browser. Click "Mailbox Settings" in the left hand toolbar. Step 2. Click "Cancel Mailbox" . Step 3. Choose from the three options of 3 Months, 6 Months, or 12 Months by clicking the "Select" button. Step 4. Choose your payment method and click "Confirm" .

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Reopening an Old Account

You can renew or reactivate an old account by logging in to your account on a desktop or mobile browser, and paying any outstanding balance for the months that have passed. Your mailbox number can often be retrieved if you reopen your account within 90 days. If it has passed the 90 days and you are unable to reactivate your previous account, you will be prompted to enter your payment information and add a new mailbox. Note: If your account no longer has login access or you do not see these options, please contact customer support and we will do our best to assist you.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## How to Forward Mail via USPS After Cancellation

To forward your mail via USPS after canceling your account, please file a Corrections Form 3546 with USPS. Since iPostal1 addresses are Commercial Mail Receiving Agencies (CMRA) locations, a regular change of address cannot be filed.

## My credit card is being declined or not going through, what should I do?

## How are yearly/annual plans charged?

Yearly plans renew only once a year. When you subscribe annually, youâ€™ll pay for ten months and receive two months free. This discount is included in the total price you pay. Example: Yearly Green Plan 30 = $99 per year. Monthly Green Plan 30 starts at $9.99 per month = $119.88 per year. Note: Our $99 annual subscription plan saves you two months on subscription fees. Billing is automatically renewed unless you cancel your plan before the renewal date. Prepaid yearly plans are non-refundable after the first 30 days.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Why is my plan more than $9.99?

Your monthly plan varies by the plan and location you selected. All plans includes a specific amount of mail items to receive per month. You will notice separate prices for business plans, if you included a business name to your account. Pricing may vary based on your mail center location. The majority of our locations are Standard locations and start at the $9.99 price. Standard , Select , Premium , or Prestige locations each have different starting prices . Starting price for Virtual Mailing Address Plans (Standard location): Green - $9.99 per month (30 mail items per month) Blue - $14.99 per month (60 mail items per month) Silver - $24.99 per month (120 mail items per month) Gold - $39.99 per month (240 mail items per month) Starting price for Virtual Business Address Plans (Standard location): Business Green - $14.99 per month (30 mail items per month) Business Blue - $19.99 per month (60 mail items per month) Business Silver - $29.99 per month (120 mail items per month) Business Gold - $44.99 per month (240 mail items per month) Note: You may notice tax is charged for your mailbox account, if your mail center is in Canada or located in a state that charges tax for mailbox services.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Why is the Mailbox Monthly Fee not the Same at all Locations?

Starting prices based addre ss type: Select Address: +$10 Premium Address: +$20 Prestige Address: +$30

## Why do I have to pay to pick up my Mail?

Since digital mailboxes are not self-service like physical mailboxes, some mail centers charge a nominal fee for processing and retrieving your mail when you come in to pick it up. Pick up fees are charged, depending on the mail item type. Note: To view your locations pick up fees on iPostal1.com , click on "Locations" on the top toolbar, s elect your location and click on "More Details".

## PayPal Payment Overview

Paying with PayPal is a convenient and secure way to make payments for your online mailbox. Your Paypal information will be requested during checkout. When paying with PayPal, y ou will be required to maintain a minimum balance above $20.00 on your account. When the account drops below the minimum of $20.00 , you are automatically charged to maintain a balance for the account minimum. T his ensures that your subscription and account will remain active. Not e: You will be prompted to agree to the Paypal Terms of Agreement before signing up. Your first payment will include the subscription fee and $25 toward your Paypal balance . Any unused PayPal funds is refundable, if you choose to close your account in the future. Recharge options: $20, $25, $50 and $100.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## PayPal Minimum Balance

Your PayPal Account requires a minimum $20 balance. When your account falls below $20, your account will renew for $20. The PayPal Terms of Agreement before sign up requires all customers to agree to the minimum balance requirement.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Why did I get an alert that I need to add funds to my PayPal account?

You will usually receive a notification with a link to add funds to your PayPal account, if your mail center is completing a task for your mail items and your account balance is not enough to cover the cost of the task. Your task will be processed after you have updated your payment method.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## I cancelled my account, when will I be refunded for my PayPal Balance?

If you choose to cancel your iPostal1 Mailbox account, the remainder of the PayPal balance will be returned to your PayPal account with 5-7 business days.

(on request, weekly, bi-weekly, monthly) Personal Digital Mailbox - access online or with an app to manage mail. Your choice of carriers, ship dates, speed and service level. Discard or dipose mail items. Preparation of commercial invoice. (for international shipments) Consolidation of letters into one package for forwarding. Note: Pickup fees are due at the time of picking up your mail and it is charged to the payment method on file for your account. To view your locations pickup pricing: Step 1. Go to iPostal1.com . Step 2. Click on " Locations" , located on the top toolbar. Step 3. Locate your mailing address. Step 4. Click " Click for More Details" , just below to show the exact pickup price for your mail center.

## Shipping and Consolidation

We offer comprehensive shipping services from all major carriers: USPS, FedEx and UPS. When you login to your account and choose to ship your mail, you will be able to select from the levels of service and pricing that fits your needs. Shipping Prices: Our system will provide an estimated shipping quote based on your mail center, the carrier, speed of shipping, destination address and dimensional weight. A dditional fees may be applied to the quote/ regular shipping charges such as for labor and packaging materials. Consolidation Prices: No charge for any number of letters consolidated. $1.95 per package or letter-pack consolidated. $1.95 for any number of magazines consolidated. Additional charge for packaging materials may be applied. Prepaid labels are not accepted. Note: If you are shipping multiple items of various sizes together, we recommend you use the Consolidate feature, which will provide you a quote before shipping your mail items. When choosing "Consolidate and Ship", you will not see an estimated price until after your mail center weighs all of the mail items and processes the request. To view a quoted price, we recommend choosing a consolidation of mail first. When updating a shipping address, please ensure that all shipping addresses that are entered, are valid, verified and recognized by USPS to avoid any delivery issues. Storage fees will continue to be charged per mail item until the mail item is shipped. The shipping address must be a valid USPS address. International shipping varies by country.

## Check Deposit

Check deposit is a great feature that can be used to conveniently ships the checks from your iPostal1 Mailbox directly to your bank account via mail. Each check that you would like deposited will need to be scanned first, before you can proceed to request a check deposit task. Please request a scan and once this request is processed by your mail center usually within 24-48hrs, you will then be able to choose if you would like to have the check deposited. As an alternative, you can have the check shipped or picked up instead. Note: The cost for each check deposit request is $4.95, plus the cost of trackable USPS Shipping (on average $11-15). This includes up to 5 checks per check deposit request. This service is available in most locations but limited to Mail Centers in the United States. Please contact your mail center directly to see if this service is provided. If the Check Deposit feature is not clickable or grayed out, please be sure you have requested a scan first. Once your mail center has processed the scan, the Check Deposit button will be available.

## Scanning/Shredding/Bundle price

Photos of the outside of your mail items are included with your plan. If you would like to view the inside contents of your mail item, you must request a scan for each item. An additional fee is charged per scan request. Discarding of mail item is usually free of charge, if you would like to shred the mail item instead, a fee is charged for each shredding request. The fee for a single scan or shred request is $2.25 per letter, up to 10 pages, and an additional $0.25 per additional page. To save money on the cost of scanning the inside contents of your mail or shredding your mail, you can purchase a bundle. Scan and shred bundles can be purchased directly through your account and are more economical. With these prepaid bundles, you can use them as needed. Discount Bundle Prices $10.00 for 5 scans or shred orders. Save 10%* $18.00 for 10 scans or shred orders. Save 20%* $30.00 for 20 scans or shred orders. Save 33%* *up to 10 pages per order Order size = 1 envelope Note: Bundles are non-refundable but can be applied to multiple addresses on merged accounts, and they do not expire. To purchase your bundles: 1. Log in to your account and Click the purple Buy Bundles option in the Top Menu Bar. 2. Click the bundle that best suits your needs and click the Continue button.

## How often do I get charged for storage?

Storage fees are charged after the initial free storage period for a mail item has expired, each mail item has their own expiration date. To avoid storage fees, it is important to select an action for your mail items such as discard, shred, shipping or pickup. If no action is taken and the free storage period has expired, a storage fee is charged based on the mail item type. Note: The larger the mail item, the less amount of storage time is given, as it is taking up more space at your mail center location. Free storage period: â— Letters, large Envelopes, Magazines and Postcards: 30 FREE days. â— Small package: 10 FREE days. â— Large packages: 5 FREE days. Storage Fees: â— Letters, Large Envelopes, Magazines, Postcards: $1.10 per mail item (every 30 days) â— Packages 12"x12"x12"and under or equivalent: $1.10 per pound* (every 30 days) â— Packages 12"x12"x12" to 24"x17"x12" or equivalent: $1.10 per pound* (every 10 days) â— Packages 24"x17"x12" and above or equivalent: $1.10 per pound* (every 5 days) *Greater of actual weight or dimensional weigh t.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## I picked up my mail, why did I get storage fees?

To prevent unnecessary storage fees, please schedule a pickup in advance of picking up your mail. Your mail center will process the pickup you created at the time of you picking up. If the mail items were not updated when you picked up your mail, and it is still showing in your inbox, your account will continue to generate storage fees. Please contact your mail center to remove these mail items from your account. Note: If you would like to request a retroactive storage refund, please contact us directly. All storage refunds need to be approved by your mail center before processing.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## When was I informed of storage fees?

An email notification is sent to you 3 days in advance, before the mail item expires, notifying you that a storage fee will be incurred soon, if no action is taken for the mail items. This allows you time to take action on your mail items by: Shipping, Picking up, Discarding or Shredding. Expiration date: You can view the expiration date for each mail item, when signed in to your account. The expiration date is located towards the center of the page and to the right of the mail item image.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## How long can I hold mail or packages in my mailbox?

You receive 30 days free storage for all letters, magazines, letter packs. Packages are given 5 - 10 days, depending on the size. Once your expiration date is expired, you will begin to be charged storage. Letters and flat mail are charged $1.10/item per month. Packages that exceed 1,728 cubic inches (equivalent to 12" x 12" x 12") are given 10 days free storage. Packages that exceed 4,895 cubic inches (equivalent to 24" x 17" x 12") are given 5 days free storage. Packages are charged $1.10/pound* per every 5, 10, or 30 days - According to the size and storage time frame allotted to the package. * Greater of actual weight or dimensional weight. Note: To avoid storage charges please select an action such as recycle, shred, forward, or pick up mail items within your free storage period. Once the free storage period has exceeded, all storage fees will be applied automatically. You do not have to do anything extra in your account. Your mail center will automatically hold your mail items.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Can I extend my storage time after my free storage time expired?

Storage time is automatically extended after your expiration date has been expired, your mail center will hold your mail items at a small fee. You do not need to do anything extra on your account. You will be charged storage fees automatically until the mail item is picked up, shipped, discarded or shredded. Note : Please ensure you select an action for your mail items on time, to avoid additional storage fees.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## How to request a refund

If you qualify and would like to request a refund, please contact customer support directly and an agent will be happy to assist you. All refunds must be approved before processing. Subscription: If your account has been cancelled within the first 30 days of sign up and has been unused, you may be eligible to request a refund of your subscription fee. Prepaid yearly plans are non-refundable after the first 30 days. Notary fees are non refundable. Other Refunds: Storage, Shipping and other service refunds will need to be approved by your mail center location before we can proceed with processing the refund. Online Notary: Notary fees via proof.com are non refundable. Scan and Shred Bundles: Unused credits from a scan or shred bundles are non refundable.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Can my Scan/Shred bundle be refunded?

Unfortunately, Scan/Shred bundle purchases are non-refundable. However, these credits do not expire and can be used across merged accounts.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Can my Phone/Fax credits be refund?

Phone and Fax credits are non-refundable, however, d uring your initial sign up, iPostal1 provides a $10 in Phone/Fax credits to start out with after you sign up for your virtual plan.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Can the rest of my annual subscription be refunded?

If you choose to close your account within the first 30 days of opening and your mailbox has not been used for any reason, you may be eligible for a refund of your . Prepaid yearly plans are non-refundable after the first 30 days. Billing is automatically renewed unless you cancel your plan before the renewal date.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## When will I receive my refund?

If you qualify for a refund for your subscription fees and you have already requested a refund with a customer support agent, it will generally take 3-5 business days to process. All other refunds including storage or shipping refunds, will need to be approved first by your mail center, before processing and can take longer at times.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Why am I being charged if I closed my account?

If you have cancelled your iPostal1 mailbox account and there are still charges being withdrawn from your account, we recommend contacting a customer support agent to resolve this matter promptly. They will be able to verify your account status and address any billing issues.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Can we have multiple Logins for each user?

Only one login is allowed per account. In order for other recipients to login to the iPostal1 account, you must share your login credentials for the account.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Can I receive mail for more than one business name?

Only one business name is allowed per mailbox account. If you signed up for a business account you are allowed up to 1 business name. If you would like to receive mail for an additional business, you will be required to open a separate mailbox number (at the same address or any other iPostal1 address) for each additional business name, including an LLC or DBA. Note: You can choose to open a second account at your current mail center location or choose any other iPostal1 location.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Can I use the same 1583 Form for Multiple Locations?

To comply with USPS regulations, you must file a new 1583 form for each mailbox location you open. A discount is available when using the online notary service for multiple locations.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Do I need to create a new login for a second mailbox?

You can use the same login to access all mailboxes at all locations. Simply add the new mailbox within your account. If you may need assistance with merging accounts, please contact customer support directly.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Where can I find my virtual mailing address?

Your virtual mailing address can be found after signing in to your account. It is located at the top right hand toolbar. If you signed up for multiple accounts, click on the small dropdown arrow located immediately to the right of your address and you'll be able to view your additional address.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## How to write my new address

You will receive a street address and a mailbox number that is unique. When sharing your address and sending mail to your location, it is important to list your full mailbox number and suite number (if applicable) to ensure your mail arrives to your inbox. You can locate your full address in your welcome email after your account has been approved. Go to your Inbox and click on " Select Locations" to see how to write all your addresses.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Is mail automatically forwarded to my new address?

Mail and packages are not automatically forwarded to your new mailing address. Your virtual mailing address will only be available to the contacts and senders that you update. If you would like all mail to be forwarded to your new mailing address, you will need to fill out a separate USPS form. Once your account is fully approved by your mail center, we recommend visiting your local post office to fill out the form. Another option is to simply tell your contacts directly that your address has changed. This is what most customers do that want most of their mail still coming to their home address, and want the iPostal1 address to be there for business use. To ensure you receive mail to your new mailing address, after your account is fully approved: 1. Inform your senders and contacts of your new address. 2. File a Temporary Change of Address form with your local post office. Note: USPS will forward all First Class mail to your new address for 6 months at no charge and can be renewed for another 6 months. We do not recommend filing a Permanent Change of Address form with the USPS. If you file a Permanent Change of Address Form, the USPS will not forward mail from your iPostal1 mailing address to a new address later on. Any permanent address change can't be reverted if you would ever need to move your mail from iPostal1 to another place.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Can I use this address to register my business, at a bank or to get a driver's license, or get insurance?

Many customers have used our virtual mail address to register their businesses, at a bank or for the Department of Motor Vehicles/DMV. The vast majority of states permit the use of virtual mailing address, but the laws may vary by state and can change periodically. Please check the local laws to determine what's permissible. Note: Please ensure that your account is fully approved before using your mail center address. Images of your mail center address cannot be used.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Can I change my iPostal1 mail center address/ location?

You will be able to request for your account to be transferred to another mail center location. Please note when you change your address, you we will need to provide an updated notarized USPS Form 1583. Each location is priced differently, and additional fees may apply when transferring to a new location. To switch to a different iPostal1 address, please follow these steps: 1. Empty your Inbox by discarding, shredding, shipping, or picking up any remaining mail items. We cannot transfer you until your Inbox is empty. 2. Contact iPostal1 customer support directly to begin the transfer process. 3 . Submit a new, notarized Form 1583 , which includes your new location's information, once you have been transferred. You must notarize online using proof.com . You can visit your mail center directly if notary service is available at your location. Please contact your mail center ahead of time for more details. 4. Provide your new address to your senders once your account is fully approved and update them accordingly. 5. File a Temporary Change of Address form with the USPS to redirect your future mail.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Where does my mail go if I cancel my account?

If you have filed a "Temporary Change of Address form" with your post office, you can easily cancel the temporary address change and file a new one. To correct or modify a change of address order, you can use the "USPS Form 3546". I f you have filed a Permanent Change of Address form, you will need to inform your senders individually that your address has changed. Note: If no forwarding option is filed, any new mail that is received at your mail center will be returned to sender.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Can I still have mail come to my house if I have an iPostal1 Virtual Address?

Your mail can still come to your house. Many customers use the iPostal1 address as an additional address. If you do not fill out a Change of Address form with USPS, your mail coming to your home will not be affected.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you may need a rental agreement or proof of address letter, we recommend using your iPostal1 invoice as valid documentation or you can choose to use your welcome email that is sent after your account is approved. ## Can I have mail or a package delivered at another location?

If you are traveling and need to have mail delivered to another address, you will be required to add a new location and submit the required documents for each location. ## My mail center location has been moved or closed

If your iPostal1 digital mailbox address location has changed or been moved for any reason, you must complete the required process to receive mail at your new address. Please log in to your digital mailbox to complete the process to avoid a delay in receiving your mail. To begin receiving mail: You will receive a notification via email with details on how to proceed. Please provide your new address to your senders, as it is listed above. If you want any mail to be forwarded from your prior address, per iPostal1 Terms of Service, please contact your prior location and arrange to pay for postage in advance. Otherwise mail will be returned to sender or discarded. You may submit a USPS 3546 Correction Form at any U.S. Post Office to redirect your future mail. This form must be completed on paper, as it cannot be submitted online. Note: Check your email for your new mail center address and mailbox number.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## How does Virtual Office Plan work?

When you select a virtual office plan, you will be prompted to choose a local or toll-free phone and fax number after you log in to your personal Digital Mailbox. You can receive incoming calls to this virtual number and the call will automatically be forwarded to the phone number of your choice. You can receive and review fax conveniently from within your account. Your forwarding number can easily be changed at any time. You'll have an option to customize how many times the phone will ring before being forwarded to your voicemail. You can set your own voice message or type in the wording for a professional automated message. You'll receive a notification when a voicemail is received. You can easily listen to your voice messages from the iPostal1 app or your iPostal1 online mailbox. Outgoing fax is not a supported feature at this time. When you receive a call to your virtual phone number, the Caller ID will display your virtual phone number. This helps you to easily recognize these calls. We suggest saving your virtual phone number as a contact to allow you to quickly identify the source of the call. Note: Some locations may offer office space rental at a separate fee. This plan does not include a physical office space.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## What is included in a Virtual Office plan and how does it work

When choosing a virtual office plan, you will receive a mailing address for your business, along with all the features of our Digital Mailbox service. What makes our Virtual Office plans different, is that you also get a phone line with call forwarding and voicemail capabilities, so you can have a business number linked to your mailing address and avoid using your personal phone for business. Conference and meeting rooms are not part of your iPostal1 plan but may be offered at your location at an additional fee. Please contact your mail center directly for more information on additional services that they may offer. If you sign up for our Virtual Office plan, you receive: Virtual mailing address. Phone forwarding. Voice mail messaging with personal greeting. A dedicated electronic fax placed into your digital mailbox as a PDF. Note: Phone forwarding at iPostal1 addresses outside the U.S s available on a limited basis.

Virtual Office plans start at $39.99 per month. This includes a real physical street address, complete Digital Mailbox service, phone forwarding, voice mail messaging, and fax line. Competitive rates per call and per fax apply.

Please contact your mail center directly to see if fax service is provided. You can find your locations fax number in the "Contact Us" page, when logged into your dashboard. Pricing to receive a fax: $2.00 each fax, up to 6 pages $0.25 each additional page Note: You can choose to upgrade to a virtual office plan which includes virtual fax at an additional fee. Your Form 1583 cannot be faxed or emailed to your location.

Your Virtual Office Phone line can take incoming calls and messages only and cannot be used to make outgoing phone calls.

## How much mail can I receive every month?

Your selected plan level determines how much mail you can receive each month. This includes all types of mail items from letters to packages. Monthly Limit per Plan: Green Plan - 30 mail items per month. Blue Plan - 60 mail items per month. Silver Plan - 120 mail items per month. Gold Plan - 240 mail items per month. Note: An additional fee of $.35 per mail item, will be applied for e a ch additional mail item that exceeds your monthly plan limit. You can always upgrade your plan at any time, if needed.

## Can I receive large packages and are there any extra fees?

You can receive large packages but if you plan on receiving mail larger than 100 lbs., it is helpful to contact your mail center location to make sure they will be able to accommodate a package of that size. Pick up fee: The fee to pick up the package can vary by location but can usually be from $1 - $7. Please contact your mail center directly for more information. S torage fees : Depending on the package size, each package is given 5 - 10 days of free storage. After that, they are charged $1.10 per pound every 30 days. Box image : If you request a box image, a fee of $3.95 will be charged for opening the package and taking images of the inside contents. To find your mail center contact information: Sign in to your account on a desktop or mobile browser. Locate the left toolbar on your account. Click: "Support Center" . Click: "Contact Us" .

## Can I receive mail addressed to other people?

If you receive mail under another name that is not listed on your account, the mail item will be returned to sender. Please reach out to customer support for assistance with adding an additional recipient. Some l ocations in Canada are limited to 1 customer name per account. If your account is located in the U.S., t he USPS requires a notarized USPS form 1583 and 2 acceptable forms of identification for any person or additional name that will be receiving mail to your account. If your account is located outside of the U.S., the requirements may be different. Note: Personal accounts are allowed up to 6 recipients in total, including the account holder. Business accounts are allowed up to 1 business name and 6 recipient names in total, including the account holder. Each additional recipient will need to submit the required documents and must be approved before they can begin to receive mail.

## Can I Change my Plan in the future?

You may change your monthly plan at any time, effective the next billing period. However, you may not change from a yearly plan to a monthly plan until the yearly billing period ends. Monthly plans can be upgraded to any other plan, including a yearly plan. Yearly plans can be upgraded to another yearly plan that allows for more mail items per month.

## Are scans included in my subscription plan?

The images of the outside of your mail items are viewable in your inbox and is included free of charge, up to the monthly limit of the plan that you choose. You may request a scan of the inside contents for any mail item for a small additional fee. Scanning bundles are available at discounted prices. For as low as $9.99 per month, you get all the benefits of viewing and managing your mail with an app from wherever you find yourself. This is a great value (more convenience and more features for a lot less than renting a PO Box). We keep your monthly cost low by charging for additional services only when you request them, this way you only pay for what you use. Note: For full details on iPostal1 services and pricing, see our "Pricing" pages. You will find services with fees listed under 'Optional Services'.

## Is forwarding mail included in the subscription and how much will it cost?

The cost of forwarding is not included in any subscription plan. Each mail item that you request to ship, will be charged separately. The price is determined by the mail item type, weight/ dimensions, carrier and shipping speed. Prices are set by your mail center. iPostal1 shows real-time shipping prices for any shipment you make by carrier (UPS, FedEx, USPS) and by level of service (overnight, 2-day, ground, etc.), and you choose the shipping that best meets your budget and timing needs. Note: You can choose to consolidate all mail items into one package to save on shipping. Shipping carriers and international shipping varies by location.

If you have multiple business names, a separate mailbox plan will be required for each business name. The USPS requires all accounts to have an account owner name for verification purposes. ## What are my options for the mail items in my account?

You can perform several actions for the mail in your account. Choose one of these alternatives for your mail, if no action is taken within your free storage period, y our account will continue to generate storage fees. You are allowed up to 30 days for letters and postcards and 5-10 days for packages depending on the size. Here are some of the things you can do with your mail: Shipping: We offer comprehensive shipping services from all major carriers: USPS, FedEx, and UPS. You can select from different levels of service and pricing that fits your needs. The system provides an estimated shipping quote based on various factors such as carrier, speed of shipping, destination address, and dimensional weight. Consolidate and Ship: This option allows your mail center to combine all selected mail items into one package and ship it to the destination you specify using your preferred shipping option. This saves time and money by avoiding separate shipment requests for each individual mail item. You will not see an estimated price until after your mail center weighs all the mail items and processes the request. Discard: You can discard unwanted mail free of charge. Your mail center will dispose of the unwanted mail items and they will be deleted from your inbox. If your mail items are important, consider choosing the mail shredding option instead. Pick Ups: You can pick up mail at your mail center address during business hours. It is recommended to schedule a pickup using the iPostal1 app for the best service. A small fee may be charged at the time of picking up. Shred: You can choose to shred a mail item, and your mail center will open the letter and shred the contents. The fee to shred is $2.25 per letter, including up to 10 pages, with an additional charge for more pages. Scan: You can request a scan of the inside contents of your mail items and view the images from the iPostal1 app. The charge for scanning is $2.25 for the first 10 pages of each letter and $0.25 for each additional page. Box Image: Photos of the inside of your package can be requested. When requesting this service, your mail center will open your package and take a picture of the inside contents. Additional fees apply for viewing the inside contents.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Do you automatically open and scan my mail?

Mail is kept secure and confidential, w hen items arrive you will be notified via email or push notifications via our free iPostal1 App. We open your mail only if you specifically request us to scan the contents. We open packages only when you request us to take a picture of package content, or in order to ensure compliance with shipping regulations. Note: You can choose the auto-scan feature in which all letters that are received to your account are automatically requested for a content scan. This additional feature is only for letters and does not include boxes and packages.

## Can Someone else pick up my mail?

Anyone handling mail in your account is required to be listed on as an additional recipient. Some locations in Canada are limited to 1 recipient at this time. If your mail center is located in the U.S . , the additional recipient must submit a notarized Form 1583 and Two forms of ID. F or assistance with adding an additional person to your account for pick up and to begin the notary session online, please contact customer support. The form 1583 can also be notarized at your mail center, if notary service is available and if the additional recipient has U.S. documents. Please contact your location for more information. We recommend informing your mail center of an alternate person collecting your mail and confirming their guidelines for this arrangement. Note: Some locations outside of the U.S. may have different requirements and some locations in Canada are limited to 1 name per account.

## My mail arrived to my location but I don't see it in my account yet.

Many of our mail center locations upload mail once per day and may wait until a certain time of day to upload all mail items. If you received a delivery confirmation that your mail item was delivered from the carrier, your mail center may not have had the opportunity to upload items for the day. W e recommend contacting your mail center directly to see if they can expedite uploading the item to your account. To avoid delays in receiving mail items: Your account must be fully active. All mail should include your full name or business name and full address including your mailbox number. Note: If you suspect that your mail item is lost, please contact your mail center directly for assistance. Each mail center manages its own mail, and they will be able to provide you with more information and support regarding your lost mail.

## What should I do about Junk mail?

Most mail center locations will carefully sort out and recycle or discard all junk mail, such as flyers, circulars, advertising, and catalogs that are classified by the USPS as Standard Mail. When junk mail is discarded before hand, it does not count toward your items per month received. Contact your mail center directly for more details. If you receive any unsolicited junk mail that is uploaded to your account, you may choose to discard it at no additional charge. Discarding mail that is already inserted is an included feature at no extra cost. Note: You can choose to subscribe to our App based service to stop junk mail at an additional fee of $9.99 for 3 months. To find more information or to sign up for iStopMail, login to your account and locate iStopMail on the left toolbar.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## When will I receive the shipment I requested?

Shipments are sent based on the carrier and timeline that you choose and your destination address. Many mail centers offer all levels of shipping services from USPS, FedEx and UPS. You will only receive a tracking number, if you select a trackable shipping method. Your tracking number will usually include a delivery date. For more information on the status of your shipping or consolidate and ship, please contact your location directly. Note: Tracking is not included for USPS standard/single letters and USPS First Class Mail. If you are shipping time sensitive or important mail, we recommend choosing a trackable shipping method.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Why haven't I received any mail yet?

To begin receiving mail to your mail center address, your account and documents must be fully approved by your mail center location. I f your account is not yet approved, mail items will be returned to the sender according to USPS regulations. USPS delivers mail daily and Mail centers upload mail once per day. If you are waiting for mail that hasn't arrived, please contact the sender, to confirm that your mail was shipped to the correct address. Ensure that your exact name, business name and mailbox number is correctly included in your address.

They are generated only for mail item shipped via USPS Priority or above. If you have selected a lower service such as USPS First Class or below, you will not receive a tracking number. T o locate a tracking number: 1. Log in to your account. 2. Click on your "Username" dropdown arrow, located on the top right of your account. 3. Click "Transactions" to view your invoices and l ocate the invoice. 4. Click "View Detail" , the tracking number will be located at the bottom of the details page.

The exact processing time depends on when the task was requested and your mail centers business days and hours. Processing time may not including weekends and holidays. ## How does "Consolidate and Ship" work?

The "Consolidate and Ship" option is a one-step request that allows your mail center to consolidate all mail items into one package and ship it to the destination you specify, using your preferred shipping option. This feature saves time and money; you do not have to create a separate shipment request for each individual mail item. When choosing "Consolidate and Ship", you will not see an estimated price until after your mail center weighs all of the mail items and processes the request. To view a quoted price before shipping, we recommend choosing a Consolidation of mail first. If you need to make changes to a consolidated mail item, please contact your mail center directly. Mail from 2 different mailbox accounts cannot be consolidated into to one. Note: The weight calculated is not the actual weight of the mail item, it is the dimensional weight used for shipping purposes.

Shipping insurance is offered when you create your shipping request in your account. If you are shipping your mail within the domestic U.S. or internationally, t he maximum insurance value you can purchase is $2,500 per package. Additional insurance fo r shipping: $4.00 for each $100 of insurance requested.
