## Inserting Mail

Follow these steps the first time you use the USZoom Utility App. Step 1. Search for the customer Select the insert icon. Choose a Recipient by entering the name or mailbox number into the search bar. The account information populates, including a company name on the account. Click to confirm the correct account. Step 2. Take a clear picture Take a clean, uncluttered close up picture of the outside of the item. Include all information which will benefit the customer, such as sender information and tracking number. Click "Done" to capture the picture. Step 3. Select the mail item type Letters: Click "Insert mail" . Choose the mail type: Large Envelopes, Letter Packs, Magazines: Add the weight. Packages: Select the mail type. Add the weight and all 3 dimensions. Step 4. Insert the mail item and label with the new mail ID Click "Insert mail" . A message stating "Insert succeeded!" with a Mail ID number appears. Write the Mail ID number on the front of the mail item for future reference. The customer is now alerted that they have received a new mail item. Step 5. Insert other mail items for the same customer As a time-saving measure, the system asks you: â€œDo you want to insert another mail item into the same box number?â€ and will automatically pull up your camera to do this. If your next item is for the same customer, click "Yes" . Otherwise, click "No" . If no , the Utility App will return to the "Choose Recipient" screen. Click here to download

## Consolidate and Ship

Below will walk you through the steps to complete a consolidate and shipping request. Log into your USZoom Utility App using your credentials. Go to Tasks Tile. Select the consolidate and shipping task you would like to process. Step 1. Locate the mail items that are listed on the task and put them together in a new envelope or box. Click 'Next'. Step 2. Confirm the mail item type, weigh the envelope or box containing all of the mail items and enter the new weight and dimensions if applicable. Click the checkbox to certify the envelope contains documents only, if applicable then click 'Next. Click on 'Confirm order'. Step 3. Select the customers preferred shipping method. Step 4. Confirm the order. Once confirmed you will print the shipping label and affix it to the front of the item. Click here to download

## How does mail storage work?

Recipients are charged for mail storage based on the weight of the mail item. On our website, you will see the pricing breakdown of storage by weight and type of mail. It's important to note that the charge is based on the dimensional weight and not the actual weight of the item. Letters, Large Envelopes, Magazines, Postcards: CA $3.99/item per month All soft packages/letter packs: CA $1.50/kilo* per month Boxes under 30x30x30 (cm) or equivalent: CA$1.50/kilo* per month Packages 30x30x30 (cm) to 60x40x30(cm) or equivalent: CA $1.50/kilo* per 10 days Packages at or over 60x40x30 (cm) or equivalent: CA$1.50/kilo* per 5 days *Greater of actual weight or dimensional weight Entering the correct weight and dimensions will ensure that the mail is properly accounted for. Mail will be charged for storage until the recipient requests to Ship, Discard, Shred or Pickup. Taking the time to process Pickup tasks when the recipient arrives will ensure that the storage fees are correct.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## What happens if a Recipient's Credit Card Declines in a Task?

Our System always ensures that the credit card on file for a recipient is valid when a payment is processed. If a recipient's credit card declines during a task, the system will send an alert to the recipient.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## How to decline a task?

To decline a task: 1. Click on "Tasks" . 2. Locate the task that you would like to decline. S elect the red "Decline Task" option in the bottom left corner. 3. You'll then be prompted to select a reason for declining, which will be emailed to the customer. Click "Done" . Our system will automatically notify the customer, and the mail item status will be updated accordingly.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## What should I do if I put a letter in the wrong recipient's mailbox?

If you need to update the mailbox that mail was inserted for, please create a support ticket and be sure to include both customer's names, mailbox numbers and mail item number to handle this request.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Mail Received for a recipient not appearing on the app

Mail will only be accepted for customers who are recognized and listed in the mobile app. Any mail received for a customer without an active account visible in the iPostal1 app will be returned to the sender. Note: To view the names associated to a mailbox account, click on "Reports" and select the mailbox number or customer.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## How long do I hold on to mail for an active customer?

Mail should be held for the life of the account. Customers are notified via email when free storage on mail items will expire and are reminded that an action has to be taken on the mail item to avoid storage fees.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Lost Mail

In the rare case that something happens, and a mail item is missing or you can't find a customer's mail item, please follow the correct steps. Proceed with the following steps: Check every file folder for your iPostal1 clients. Each mail item has a unique mail ID and will continue to incur storage charges as long as it remains in the customer's mailbox. For assistance with reporting the lost mail item and updating the mail status, please create a support ticket and be sure to include the customers name, suite number and mail item number to handle this request. Be sure to include any helpful details you know about the lost mail item.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## What happens if I donâ€™t process a mail pickup on the Utility App when the Recipient Walks In?

The mail items will remain in the recipient's inbox and accrue storage fees. It is best if the pickup is processed the day the recipient arrives to avoid any storage fees. If a pickup is not processed for any reason please create a support ticket, be sure to provide the customers suite number and mail ID.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Cannot find a pickup task for a customer

If a customer comes to the store to pick up without scheduling online, please follow the steps below to create and process a pickup for the customer. Ask for ID to verify the customers identity. Open your USZoom Utility App and log in. Step 1. Create the pickup: 1. Tap on "Pickups" . Choose "+Create Pickup" . 2. Enter the name or mailbox number of recipient into the search bar. 3. Tap "Select from list" then select specific mail items or choose "Select all" and tap on "Enter". 4. A confirmation screen will appear with the selected mail items. Tap on "Create Pickup" . 5 . The pickup task now appears, showing the mail items that need to be pulled from the customers mailbox and handed to the customer. Step 2. Process the pickup: 1. Click "Add Signature". 2. Have the customer sign that they have picked up their mail and tap on "Done" . 3. Tap on "Complete" . The customer will be charged, the mail items will update, and the customer's signature will be stored. 4. Hand mail to the customer.

## What If the recipient's credit card didn't go through when processing a Pickup?

Our system will automatically process customers credit card in real-time. If the customer has attempted to enter their credit card details and it is not being accepted by the system, we recommend they try a different credit card. If their payment is being denied or declined, it is best for them to contact their bank or financial institution to determine the issue. It is important to process the pickup before handing the mail item to the customer to ensure the payment is collected.

## Customer request to add an additional mail item to a task

Once a customer creates a shipping task, we cannot add additional mail items or modify any details. If a customer wants to add items or consolidate shipments, the customer must cancel the request in their account. They can then submit a new request that includes all desired mail items and select their preferred shipping method and price.

## Understanding recipient's shipping options

Recipient's have 2 options to ship there mail items. As they walk through creating the request, they are shown the shipping options available. The customer can choose to ship 1 mail item at a time by selecting "Create a Shipment" or they can choose to ship multiple mail items at once by choosing "Consolidate and Ship" . " Create a Shipment" - Customers see specific price quotes to ship the mail item. This is because there are clear weight and dimensions for the single package/letter. The customer will choose a shipping method, speed and price. (customer view) "Consolidate and Ship" - These requests have General Shipping Options with no price or N/A, as the weight of the item isn't yet determined in the system until all items are combined and weighed. Customers will see this note when choosing a shipping method. (Customer view) Additional Shipping Options: (Customer view) Shipping Insurance - Shipping insurance is not included but may be purchased the maximum insurance value a customer can purchase is CA $3,500 per package. Additional Insurance for shipping: CA$5.49 for each $100 of insurance requested. Require Signature - The customer has the option to require a signature when the mail item is delivered by the carrier, you do not have to do anything extra if the customers selects this. Remove the Invoice - If the customer selects this option, you can open the mail item, remove the receipt/invoice and re-seal the package. Special Instructions - Some customer's may enter special instructions in the space provided. If you have a question or need clarification on these instructions, please contact support. Once the task is submitted by the customer: It's important to follow the recipient's instructions for a shipment. If you have any questions for the recipient, please contact support. Note: Auto-ship tasks are pre-selected by the customer. They choose the day of the week and the frequency they'd like the task to occur. These tasks will generate automatically and appear in your dashboard to-do list, just like any regular task.

## Do Not Ship List

DO NOT SHIP Combustible or Flammable Items: Paints, oils, lighters, perfume, nail polish, alcohol. Pressurized Cans: Hair spray, shaving cream, spray cans of any type. Hazardous Materials: Matches, chemicals, explosives, fuels, fertilizers. Firearms/Ammunitions. Medications: Prescription & veterinary medications prohibited. Non-prescription medications are restricted. Agricultural Products: Tobacco products of any kind including cigars, cigarettes, tobacco leaves, chewing tobacco, plants, and seeds. Marijuana Food-Drink that are Perishable foods. Money and Valuables: Cash, currency, money orders, cashiers' checks, bank drafts, bearer bonds and collectible stamps and coins. Jewelry and precious stones Purolatorâ€™s standard liability coverage for loss or damage is CA $100 per shipment. You can declare a higher value for an extra fee, their coverage for jewelryâ€”particularly precious metals and stonesâ€”is usually excluded entirely under the â€œAt Shipperâ€™s Riskâ€. Animals and products made with animal skins (furs) Chemicals of any kind Lottery tickets and gambling devices Liquids Pornography Lock picking devices Suspicious substances Unlabeled items that cannot be identified

Click "Select from list" , then select specific mail items or choose "Select all" if the customer is pickup all of the mail items. 4. A confirmation screen appears with the list of mail items selected. Click "Create pickup" . 5. The pickup task now appears, showing the mail items that the customer is picking up. Click "Add Signature" and have the customer sign. 6. Select "Done" and "Complete" . You will see confirmation message and you can now hand the mail to the customer. ## Single Letter Rate tasks

Our system does not ge nerate a label for Single-Letter rate shipping tasks. When processing a single letter rate task, domestic or international, you are simply shipping the mail item with a stamp. Note: All single letter rate envelopes should weigh less than 30g and the envelope should be no larger than 9.6 inches x 6.1 inches x 0.2 inches, with out a clasp. To process Single-Letter rate: Place the item into a slightly larger envelope. Write the address on the front of the envelope. Attach the stamp in the upper right corner. Send it in the outgoing mail.

Identity Verification: F orm 1583, Enrollment form, Verification Process After signing up, you will be assigned a personal mailbox number. You will be prompted to proceed based on the location of your mail center: locations in the U.S. you will proceed to fill out a USPS Form 1583 that authorizes your digital mailbox location to receive mail on your behalf. You will need two forms of acceptable IDs and you can then choose to notarize online or in person at the mail center location you signed up for. -To notarize online : please select online notary and follow the link that is sent to your email. ## Requirements

To open a virtual iPostal1 mailbox in the U.S., you will be need to provide the following: Valid payment method: W e accept American Express, Visa, MasterCard, and Discover and PayPal. Documents: For U.S. mailboxes, a completed form 1583 that is notarized online or completed at your mail center. For mailboxes outside of the U.S. please follow the steps in your account. Identification: 2 acceptable IDs from the list; 1 photo ID and 1 address ID (must match the name used to sign up, cannot use a nickname). Address: A current address that matches your photo ID to complete USPS Form 1583. Online session: A mobile phone or computer with strong internet connection and access to video and microphone. Note: If your mailbox location is outside of the U.S., please contact customer support, as the requirements may vary by location. If you don't have a U.S. address you must still file the USPS form 1583. You'll be required to notarize the Form 1583 using our online notary service for $25.

## Select your plan

iPostal1 offers Virtual Mailing Address plans for personal use only starting at $9.99/month, and Virtual Business Address plans to receive mail under a business name as well as for personal use, starting at $14.99/month. Each plan has four options, depending on how much mail you expect to receive each month. We offer Virtual Office plans that may be used with a business name and for personal use, and come with phone forwarding and fax, starting at $39.99/month. Get two months free on any plan when you select a Yearly plan. You may change your monthly plan at any time, effective the next billing period. Note: Yearly plans can be upgraded to another yearly plan that allows you to receive more mail items per month. However, you may not change from a yearly plan to a monthly plan until the yearly billing period ends. Most of our locations are Standard addresses that start at $9.99/month. Addresses in prestigious buildings or in locations where costs and demand are higher, may cost more according to the address type: Select +$10; Premium +$20; Prestige +$30.

You can add your preferred payment method when signing in your account on a desktop or mobile browser. We accept American Express, Visa, MasterCard, and Discover. You can also select to use PayPal. Note: Renewal is automatic, whether you have a monthly or a yearly plan. If your mailbox is located in Canada, you will not be able to choose PayPal as a payment method.

## Forwarding mail to your new iPostal1 address

A change of address is recommended when youâ€™d like your mail to be redirected to your new iPostal1 address. After your account is fully approved, we recommend completing the temporary change of address in person at a Post Office near you . We have found that the online change of address system, unfortunately, USPS doesn't always recognize/accept the addresses because of the added suite number, so please complete this in person to avoid any issues or delays. Upon signup, we assign you a unique suite number to go along with the address you selected - this is to set you apart from the other customers signing up at the same location. For this reason, it is an important part of the address, along with your full name and/or business name if applicable. All of this information is required to be listed on any incoming mail. If the name, business name or mailbox number do not match, you mail may be returned to sender. Note: We recommend updating your address, after your account is fully approved by your mail center. We do not recommend filing a Permanent Change of Address form with the USPS. A Temporary Change of Address is good for 6 months and may be renewed for an additional 6 months.

## Closing an account within 30 days

If you choose to close your account within the first 30 days of opening, you may receive a refund of the mailbox rental fee if you did not use your account to receive mail or for any other purpose. Please contact iPostal1 to see if you qualify and to request a refund. Note: If you filed a Temporary Change of Address form with your Post Office, you can easily cancel the Temp address change, and file a new one. However, if you filed a Permanent Change of Address, you will need to inform your senders individually that your address has changed.

## What is a Form 1583 and why do I need one?

The USPS Form 1583 is a 'Permission Slip' that you sign to allow your mail to be processed by a third party address. Most people who sign up are new to the concept. We are happy to explain why you need one for your online mailbox. Providing your IDs, notary and signature verify that you are the one who authorizes mail to come to your account. We provide you with a pre-filled form 1583 inside of your account and easy access to an online notary. Your form 1583 is automatically uploaded to your account after the online notary session is completed. You can notarize directly at your mail center, if your location provides this service. Your location will upload your documents to your account. Please call ahead and be sure to have your required documents available when visiting your mail center. We do not accept local notaries, such as from a bank or any other personal notary. 1583 Forms cannot be notarized at the post office. Forms cannot not be uploaded or submitted via email or fax. Your mailbox location is classified by USPS as a Commercial Mail Receiving Agency (CMRA) and reports to the local Post Office. According to USPS law, in order for your Address Location to legally process mail on your behalf, the Form 1583 is required to be on file in the address location that you selected. They also will be uploading a copy of your form to the USPS database. Form 1583 must be properly signed by the mailbox renter and notarized using our online notary partner, Proof.com, or it can be signed at your mail center. Only after your mail center/ CMRA has properly reviewed the Form 1583 along with your two valid forms of ID. You will be able to begin receiving mail and request tasks for your mail, after your account is fully approved. Prior to this time, your mail and packages are subject to be returned to sender in accordance with USPS guidelines. Once your form 1583 is approved, your mail can start the journey to your iPostal1 Mailbox. Form 1583 does: Provide permission for mail to be received on behalf of the mailbox renter Verify the identity of the mailbox renter Require two acceptable IDs Require a notary or agent signature Form 1583 does not: Reroute mail from your home or business (This CAN be done through a separate 'Change of Address' Form at your local Post Office) Share/publicize your new address with the world - it is up to you to share your address with the people who send you Note: If your mailbox location is in Canada, the verification process may be different. Please contact customer support for more information.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Step by Step instructions for the Form 1583 assistant

To begin the form 1583 process, please sign into your account via a desktop computer. Click on the yellow banner across the top of your screen. Once all of the information is filled out, your form 1583 will appear in your account and can be downloaded if needed. You can then arrange to notarize remotely by choosing online notary in step 6 and follow the link that is sent to your email. If you are a US citizen and will not require international shipping, you can visit your mail center to have your documents notarized, if in person notary service is available at your mail center. Please contact the mail center you signed up for ahead of time to ensure this service is available. Other iPostal1 mail centers will not be able to notarize your documents if you have not signed up at the . Local notaries, such as banks are not allowed. Please ensure your account is fully approved before you begin using your iPostal1 address. Please contact customer support directly if you are experiencing an issue with submitting your documents. To access the form 1583 assistant: Click "Learn More", located on the yellow banner at the top of your account. Click "Edit Form 1583 Information" . If you do not see the yellow banner on your account, click on the bell icon at the top right of your screen and cancel your online notary session. Step 1. Mail Recipients for this Account: - Enter the legal name of the primary mail recipient. The name should match the name that appears on your government issued ID. If this is a business account that will receive mail for a company , please select "Yes" . You will be asked to enter your business information when you reach Step 3. If this is not a business account and you would like to add additional recipients , please select "Yes" . - Enter the full legal name and last name of your spouse/significant other . You may also enter the full legal names (first and last required) of up to three minor children. Note: If a spouse is added on this step, both the primary recipient and their spouse will need to generate a Form 1583, provide ID's, and notarize online or at your mail center if the service is available at your location. If you wish to add an additional mail recipient that is not a spouse/significant other or minor child such as a friend or employee, you will need to have that additional recipient fill out and notarize their own Form 1583. The additional recipient will be required to complete the online notary or in person at your mail center, if the service is available at your mail center location. Online notary must be used if you or your spouse live outside of the U.S., shipping internationally or have international documents. You can request a joint online notary session for a discount, by contacting iPostal1 customer support. Step 2. Your Address - As listed on your government-issued ID: Enter your home address as it appears on your Address ID document. (not your virtual address) Entering this address is required by iPostal1 and will be used in box 6 of the form 1583. This address is not optional and will only be used in the case mail needs to be forwarded to your home for any reason. You will be asked whether you'd like to hide your email address on the form, if you have a U.S. Social Security Number, and if you will be shipping items outside of the U.S. Your mail centers address is automatically entered and will show in section 2 of the form 1583. This is the location you signed up to receive your mail at. Step 3 - Your Business Information: Select whether this is a registered business. Then, enter the requested business information below. Your business address should not be your mail center address. If you do not have a business address, please enter your home address. Step 4 - Mail Recipient Identification Documents: Select the type of photo ID that you will be providing your mail center. The Photo ID should be a valid, government-issued photo ID from the list of approved ID's. Then, select the type of address ID that you will be providing your mail center. Your address IDs must verify the home address you listed in Step 2 and be on the list of approved ID's. All ID's should be current, and not soon to expire. Step 5 - Review: Please verify that all the information listed on this page is correct. Step 6 - Notarize Form 1583 or Verification Process: Option 1 - Online Notary: Click on Continue with Online Notary to proceed, then follow the link in your email. Please make sure you select the most recent email link. Proof.com, our online notary partner, is standing by for immediate processing. This option requires a webcam or smartphone. The cost for using proof.com is $25. Your notarized form and ID's will be automatically uploaded to your account with the online notary option. Click on ' Continue with Online Notary' to proceed, then follow the link in your email . Option 2 - Mail Center Location: Some of our mail centers offer Notary services in house. If your location offers this service, you can notarize your form 1583 in person. If not, then you will have to notarize your 1583 through our online notary partner, Proof.com. This option is only available for customer with U.S. documents and who will not be shipping internationally. Note: If you are signing up from an International address and/or if you would like to ship items outside of the U.S., you are required to notarize your USPS form 1583 using the online notary, proof.com.

## Which IDs can I provide for the USPS Form 1583?

Two forms of identification are required, a Primary Photo ID and a Secondary Proof of Address ID. Your 2 IDs are required to be submitted along with your form 1583. You can notarize online, using proof.com or you can visit your mail center location, if notary service is provided at your location. Please call ahead to see if notary service is provided. If your mailbox location is outside of the U.S. please contact customer support as the requirements may be different. Only the IDs listed here are accepted by iPostal1: If you have any questions or need clarification, please contact customer support. Acceptable Photo IDs: Valid state-issued driverâ€˜s license Non-driverâ€™s identification card U.S. passport, U.S. passport card Foreign passport Matricula Consular card (Mexico) NEXUS card (Canada) Acceptable Proof of Address Documents: Current lease Mortgage or deed of trust Voter or vehicle registration card Home or vehicle insurance policy Unacceptable IDs: Social Security cards Credit cards Utility bills Birth certificates National ID Cards Bank Statements University Card U.S. Armed Forces card, Uniformed Service ID card U.S. certificate of citizenship or naturalization Identification card issued by a federally or state-recognized tribal nation (tribal identification card) Vehicle lease Note: The Primary ID must have a clear photograph of the mail recipient. International customers must use their passport as their photo ID. We accept the international equivalent of the Secondary IDs listed. Leases must be current and signed. We do not accept month to month leases. International leases require a Certified Translation. Home and car insurance policy must be current. Home and vehicle insurance document must not be expired.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Where do I add my business name?

If you selected a business plan and entered a business name in step 3 when you signed up for your mailbox, our system will automatically place your business name in box 7 on the USPS form 1583. Box 7 is the correct box for your business name. Your business name cannot replace your personal name. The USPS requires all virtual mailboxes to have a personal name as the account holder, even if you will not be receiving mail under your personal name. For business account use, you may add a total of 1 business name and 5 personal names associated with one account. Note: Each additional recipient is required to provided 2 acceptable IDs and a notarized form 1583. Each additional business name LLC or DBA requires its own separate account.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## If I am using my mailbox for business only, do I need my personal name on the 1583?

USPS requires every mailbox account with a business name, to have a personal name attached to the account for verification purposes. Even if all of your mail will only be addressed to the business name alone, your personal name, signature and IDs need to be on file. The business name will be listed in box 7. Mail can arrive addressed to your name or the business name alone, without your personal name. Note: We will not share your personal information with anyone. USPS requires that information to be on file, in order for us to legally receive mail for your account.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## How to add a spouse, minor child or additional person to my mailbox?

You can add up to 5 additional names with a personal mailbox plan in the U.S. Some locations in Canada are limited to 1 recipient. Each additional recipient you add will require their own Form 1583 and must provide 2 valid forms of ID, then complete the online notary session via proof.com. A personal plan is allowed a total of 6 recipients names or 6 personal names and 1 business name for a business account. Please contact us to begin the process with proof.com . Some locations in Canada are limited to 1 customer name at this time. If you are in the sign up process, please be sure to list additional recipients such as a spouse and any minor children who are being added to your account in step 1 of the form assistant. Since minors are not of age and do not have IDs, they are not required to file their own 1583. Some mail centers may ask for proof that a recipient is a minor. Adult children (age 18 and older) must provide their own signed and notarized Form 1583 and 2 forms of ID. Spouses and any other additional recipients over the age of 18 are also required their own form, per new regulations. Some mail center locations may offer in person notary, please contact your mail center directly for more details. If the additional recipient has international documents, they will be required to use the online notary Proof.com . To add an additional name and your account is already active and approved: 1. Please contact customer support for assistance. 2. Submit the required documents and complete the online notary session. 3. Contact customer support if you may need assistance with adding the required documents after completing the notary session. To add or edit additional mail recipients to your account during sign up: 1. Click on the notification bell at the top right of your account. 2. Navigate to step 1 and scroll towards the middle. 3. Click " Yes" under " Would you like to add additional mail recipient(s) to your account", then click " Next" . 4. Notarize your documents via proof.com or in person if your mail center provides this service. Please contact customer support if you would like to request a joint notary session. If you are an international customer or will be shipping internationally, you are required to notarize online via Proof.com . Note: If you already have an open account or do not see the form assistant, please contact customer support directly.

## Can I use the same 1583 form for multiple locations?

Each location and mailbox will require a separate Form 1583. You must file a new Form 1583 for each mailbox location you open. When using our convenient online notary service, the first notarization fee is $25, but if you are notarizing multiple form 1583s in the same session, the fee is $5 each for additional form, after the first. Note: Upon completing the online notary, your Form 1583 and IDâ€™s will be uploaded directly to all of your addresses, which a great time saver. Please contact iPostal1 to arrange the notary session for multiple locations. Notary fees are non refundable.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## How will I know when my USPS Form 1583 is approved?

You will receive an email from your Mail Center notifying you that your USPS Form 1583 has been approved. You can verify the approval status of your account by logging into your account and checking under 'Mailbox Settings' located on the left toolbar. There, you can see if your mailbox address is active and approved. Additionally, the yellow box inside your account, containing Form 1583 Instructions, will disappear from your screen.

## I don't have a Social Security number, but I am being asked to enter one in the Online Notary

Wait for the email with Subject: iPostal1 - Online Notary [ACTION REQUIRED] Note: Please be sure you click the link on the new email sent, to access the online notary. ## If I don't have a company, what should I write in the Form 1583?

A company name is not required to complete the Form 1583. If you did not sign up for a business plan and are not expecting mail for your business, you may leave the company information field blank on Form 1583.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## I don't have a home address, do I have to provide a home address on the form 1583?

The USPS requires a home address to be listed on the Form 1583. You will need to provide two acceptable IDs: a current photo ID and a proof of address ID that matches the address listed on your form 1583. The address on both ID's don't need to be the same but need to match the form 1583.

## Do I have to provide my current address on the form 1583?

The USPS requires your current address to be listed on the Form 1583. You will also be required to provide 2 acceptable IDs. A current photo ID and a proof of address ID, that matches your current address entered when signing up.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Does the USPS form 1583 change my address?

The USPS form 1583 does not change your address, it simply gives your mail center permission to handle mail that arrives in your name. Once your account is fully approved by your mail center, you can update your contact and file a change of address. You will be required to fill out a separate temporary change of address form with USPS to change your address so that mail is forwarded. We recommend filling out a temporary change of Address , as any permanent change of address cannot be reverted in the future.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Can I enter my mailbox address as my business address on the form 1583?

Your business address should be the actual place you conduct your business at. If you do not have a business address, you can use your home address in this section of the form 1583.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Can I file Form 1583 if I don't have a U.S. address?

You can and must file a USPS form 1583 when signing up for a virtual mailbox, even if you don't have a U.S. address. All international customers are required to submit a notarized Form 1583 using the online notary service, proof.com. Note: If your country isn't listed or can't add your ID, please contact customer support for assistance.

## Why do I have to resubmit the form 1583?

You may be asked to fill out a new form 1583 due to the following reasons: 1. Outdated Documents: If your form 1583 is expired or if any of your IDs are expired, you will be required to update the form and provided updated IDs. 2. Local Notary: If you submit the document using a local notary it will not be accepted. 3. Adding a new address: Each individual address requires a separate form 1583. 4. Mail center closed: A new form 1583 is required including your new mail center address. 5. Changing your Mail Center location: If you changed your Mail Center location, a new form is required. Note: The USPS has recently updated the Form 1583, requiring some customer with an outdated form, to submit a new, updated and notarized form to meet the U.S. Postal Service Compliance.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## I only need my business name on this account

The USPS requires every mailbox account with a business name to have a personal name attached to the account for verification purposes. Even if all of your mail will only be addressed to the business name alone, your personal name, signature, and IDs need to be on file.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Do I have to include my middle name?

You must include your full legal name including your first and last name. If your government-issued ID includes your middle name, you should list it on Form 1583 to ensure that the name matches exactly with your ID.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## I have U.S. documents but live abroad

If you are living abroad and need to ship mail internationally, itâ€™s important to understand the identification requirements to ensure a smooth shipping process. Y ou will need to provide two forms of identification. This is a standard procedure to ensure the security and legitimacy of your shipment. By following these guidelines and ensuring you have the necessary identification, you can sign up and confidently ship your mail internationally, even while living abroad. Please contact customer support if you have any questions or need assistance. Identification Requirements 1.Primary Photo ID- The first form of identification you must present is your passport. Your passport is an internationally recognized document that verifies your identity and citizenship. It serves as the primary photo ID and is essential for international shipping. Make sure your passport is valid and not expired, as an expired passport will not be accepted. 2. Secondary Form of Identification- The second form of identification should be an internationally recognized equivalent of acceptable IDs. This can include a government-issued ID card, a driverâ€™s license, or a military ID. Itâ€™s important that this secondary ID also includes your photo and is valid.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## How do I upload/submit my documents and form 1583?

If you use our online notary service, your documents are automatically uploaded and submitted, including your Form 1583 and IDs. Our online notary is secure and reliable, ensuring that your Form 1583 can be verified. If you need to upload any new or updated documents for you, your spouse or any additional recipient such as a child or employee, please contact customer support. Be sure that your spouse or additional recipient has completed the online notary session via proof.com as local notaries will not be accepted. If you live in the U.S. and have U.S documents, many mail centers will allow you to bring your IDs and Form 1583 to sign in their presence, in which case your mail center will upload your 2 acceptable IDs and form 1583 for approval. We recommend that you contact your mail center prior to arriving to ensure this service is offered. If you have already notarized a document using a local notary, it will not be accepted. If you used Proof.com to notarize your documents and do not see your documents in your account, please contact customer support. If you have received an email to upload an updated document, you can reply to the email or contact customer support directly. Note: Uploading a notarized form 1583 using a local notary is not allowed. To add, edit or delete documents such as an ID, please contact customer support and an agent will be able to assist. If you plan on visiting your mail center location, you must visit the address you signed up for, other locations will not be able to notarize your documents. Local notaries, such as banks or the post office are not allowed. Please call ahead to see if this service is provided at your location. International customers or customers who will be shipping internationally are required to notarize online, using proof.com .

## What is the cost of the online notary service?

The fee to notarize with the online notary service, proof.com with iPostal1 is: $25.00 for one notarization, whether you reside in the U.S. or in another country. If you have signed up for more than one iPostal1 address, the cost for additional notarizations completed during the same online session is as follows: $5.00 each after your first notarization, accounts 2 through 11. No charge for notarization 12 and beyond accounts. Note : Customers living outside of the U.S. who sign up for a U.S. mailing address and customers that are shipping internationally, are required to use our online notary service.

## Do I have to get the Form 1583 notarized?

The USPS requires notarization of Form 1583 to prevent identity fraud, protecting you and the mail center. iPostal1 requires you to notarize your documents online using proof.com or via your mail center if the service is available at your location. any mail centers allow you to provide your IDs and sign the form in person in their presence, where the staff can review your IDs and verify your identity, if you have U.S. documents. Some mail centers charge for this service, so please check with your mail center for more details. If you live outside of the U.S., have international documents and will be shipping internationally, you are required to use the online notary. To initiate the online notary session, please choose online notary in step 6 and follow the link in your email. A $25.00 fee will be charged for this service. Note: You cannot fill out your Form 1583 at the Post Office. Local notaries, such as banks or other personal notaries are not acceptable. Online Notary is required: If you live outside of the U.S. If you have international documents. If you are shipping to an international location. If you have U.S. documents but cannot visit your mail center in person to provide your IDs and sign the form 1583. If your mail center does not allow you to sign the form in person. Online Notary is not required: If you visit your mail center location, provide your acceptable U.S. IDs and sign the form 1583 in person.

## Can I notarize for someone else or can someone notarize for me?

For security purposes, notarization must be done by the individual who is providing their documents. You must notarize for yourself and additional recipients must notarize for themselves via proof.com's video notary session. This ensures that no one is using your information or IDs to open an account with iPostal1.

## Online Notary Requirements

The online notary is required when you sign up for a location in the U.S. and y ou do not have a Social Security Number, are using an international passport as proof of ID or if you are shipping mail internationally. A desktop or mobile device: Video, microphone and audio are needed as well as a strong internet connection and access to your email. You will receive an email to initiate the online notary session, Fee: There is a $25 fee for a single notarization, a discount is provided to notarize multiple form 1583's if it is completed in the same session. Please contact customer support to set this up. Identification: 2 acceptable IDs from the list. 1 photo ID and 1 address ID (must match the name used to complete the form 1583). Acceptable Photo IDs: Valid state-issued driver's license Non-driverâ€™s identification card U.S. permanent resident or other identification issued by U.S. Citizenship and Immigration Services U.S. passport, U.S. passport card Foreign passport (only acceptable when notarizing online) Matricula Consular card (Mexico), NEXUS card (Canada) Acceptable Proof of Address Documents: Current lease Mortgage or deed of trust Voter or vehicle registration card Home or vehicle insurance policy Unacceptable IDs: Social Security cards Credit cards Utility bills Bank statements Birth certificates University ID Cards U.S. Armed Forces card, Uniformed Service ID card U.S. certificate of citizenship or naturalization Identification card issued by a federally or state-recognized tribal nation (tribal identification card) Note: Lease must include: name, address, start date, ending date and signature pages. Deed must include: name, address and signature page. The Primary ID must have a clear photograph of the mail recipient. International customers must use their passport as their photo ID. We accept the international equivalent of the Secondary IDs listed. Only the IDs listed here are accepted by iPostal1. If you have any questions or need clarification, please contact customer support.

## Why do I have to notarize my documents again and how do I upload them?

If you have received an email to notarize your documents for a second time, here are the possible reasons: Outdated Documents: If the documents you have provided are outdated, such as your form 1583 or IDs, a new notarized form 1583 and updated IDs will be required to maintain your mailbox account. Local Notary : If you have submitted a document using a local notary, it will not be accepted for upload. Adding a new address or change of Mail Center location: The USPS requires a new notarized form 1583 and 2 acceptable IDs for each mail center address that you sign up at. If your location has moved or you are transferring to a new location your documents on file will need to be updated. Notarization Request : If you're still receiving emails to complete your online notary session and you have already notarized your form, it is likely that more than one notary session was requested multiple times. Please contact us through chat or email so we can resolve this for you. Note: If you live in the U.S. and have U.S. documents, you can choose to notarize your documents online using proof.com or you can notarize in person at your mail center, if the service is provided at your address. Please contact your mail center location beforehand to see if this service is available. If you live outside of the U.S., have international documents or will be shipping internationally, you are required to use the online notary Proof.com . To initiate a session with proof.com, please follow the prompts in your account by filling out your information. You will then have the choice to select "Continue with Online Notary" and a link will be sent to your email address to begin the session. Your documents will be submitted after you complete the online notary session.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Can I use my own notary?

Local notaries such as banks or other personal notaries are not acceptable. Your form 1583 must be signed and notarized using the online notary proof.com or you can sign and provide your documents at the physical mail center address you signed up for, if the service is available at your mail center and if you have U.S. documents. If you would like to sign your form 1583 at your mail center address, please call your mail center ahead of time to see if this service is available. Once you complete the online notary, your form will be uploaded for review. Note: If you are an international customer or will be shipping internationally, you will be required to use the online notary.

## Can I notarize at another iPostal1 location?

If you have U.S. documents and would like to notarize your documents in person, you must visit the location address you signed up for, sign the form 1583 in person and provide 2 acceptable IDs. Other iPostal1 locations will not be able to notarize, upload or approve your documents. N ot all mail center locations accept in-person signing or notary service for Form 1583. ## Why does iPostal1 require an online notary?

iPostal1 requires online notarization to prevent identity fraud and ensure secure processing of mail. While USPS mandates notarization to verify identity, iPostal1 adds the requirement for online notarization through Proof.com , especially for international customers that open an account in the U.S. or those shipping internationally. If you are a customer with U.S. documents, you may be able to notarize in person at your mail center. Please contact your mail center directly to see if the in person service is available. Note: Some locations outside of the U.S. may have different requirements.

## What will my address look like?

All our locations are approved by the USPS as a Commercial Mail Receiving Agency (CMRA). Most locations are professional retail pack and ship stores or business coworking centers in professional office buildings. To find a list of all of our address locations please visit our locations page, click on Locations, located at the top of our site, then choose the state and city or or click here . Addresses vary by location and your personal mailbox number will most often appear on the same line as the street address. Some locations are suite addresses, the suite number will appear before your mailbox number. Note: It is important to use your full name or business name and full address including your mailbox number and suite number (if applicable) to ensure your mail arrives to the correct location. Your mailbox number and suite number cannot be changed or excluded from your address. Sample address: Your full Name or Company Name 123 Main Street #1001 Philadelphia, PA 123451

## How is an address with iPostal1 different from a PO Box?

iPostal1 mail center locations are real physical street addresses at professionally staffed, secure, and full-service mail centers, which can receive mail and packages from any carrier, including UPS and FedEx. All mail is easily managed virtually, y ou do not get an actual mailbox and key. PO Box: Only accepts USPS deliveries . You cannot use a PO box to register a business. You cannot manage your mail digitally with 24/7 access from anywhere. You have to physically check your mailbox.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Will all my mail automatically be forwarded to my mailbox address?

The USPS will forward all first class mail if you file a "Change of Address" request with your local post office. Once your account is fully approved by your mail center, you can file a change of address. Please be sure it includes your full address, including your mailbox number. We recommend using the Temporary Change of Address form, good for 6 months and renewable, so that you can redirect forwarding if you need to change mailing address location in the future. A USPS Permanent Change of Address is not reversible in the future.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

After setting up your digital mailbox, you can easily request shipments and choose your preferred carrier and service level. Note: If you are planning to ship your mail internationally, you are required to use the online notary to notarize your documents.

## Technical issues on the website

If you are experiencing issues with our website such as invalid token or server error : 1. Clear Browser Cache and Cookies : Sometimes, old cookies and cached data can cause issues with website functionality. 2. Use another browser : Using another browser such as google, chrome, safari, edge or incognito/private browsing mode can help bypass some browser-related issues. 3. Check Browser Settings : Ensure that your browser is set to accept cookies and that there are no extensions blocking the website's functionality. 4. Update Browser : Make sure your browser is up-to-date to avoid compatibility issues. 5. Contact Support : If the issue persists, it may be helpful to contact our support team for further assistance.

## Technical issues in the App

## Sign Up Instructions

For verification purposes you must create the account under your legal name and address listed on your IDs. If you select a business plan, you can add your business name to your account at signup. Upon signup, you will be required to complete a online video verification process providing a drivers license or passport. Once that has been approved youâ€™ll have full access to your account and the mail that arrives at your new virtual mailing address. How to sign up: Step 1. Choose a Location and Plan. Choose a physical address from 3,500+ digital mailbox locations across the U.S. and abroad, this address will be where you will receive your mail. Then select the plan that is best for you, depending on how much mail you expect to receive. Step 2. Checkout. Provide your contact information and enter your credit card details for payments. Step 3. Online verification process. Follow the steps to complete the online verification process. The session will take 3-5 minutes to complete. We suggest using a mobile device for ease. You will be required to provide a valid drivers license or passport for verification purposes. Step 4. Redirect Your Mail after your account is fully approved. To begin receiving mail at your new address, file a Temporary Change of Address form with the Canada Post online or in person and/or notify senders directly, once your account is approved.

## Forwarding Mail to your new iPostal1 address

Upon signup, we assign you a unique suite number to go along with the address you selected - this is to set you apart from the other customers signing up at the same location. For this reason, it is an important part of the address and is required to be listed on any incoming mail. Options to forward mail: Complete a temporary change of address at your local Canada Post. Be sure to select the Temporary Change of Address option. This type of change is valid for 3 months and can be extended for an additional 3 months if needed Inform your senders of your new address. Note: We recommend updating your address only after your account has been fully approved by your mail center. See Canada Post Website for up to date information regarding price and non forwarding items. Canada Post will not forward: Parcels (for example Xpresspost TM or Regular Parcel TM) Prepaid envelopes. Newspapers and flyers delivered by other parties. Personal mail delivered to a business/institution such as an office building, a hospital, nursing home or a hotel. Mail received at a shared postal address (i.e. when the same address is used by more than 2 businesses). Mail through a privately administrated mailbox company.

## How is an address with iPostal1 different from a PO Box?

iPostal1 addresses are real physical street addresses at professionally staffed, secure, and full-service mail centers, which can receive mail and packages from any carrier, including UPS, FedEx, Amazon and more. A PO Box only accepts Canada Post deliveries. You cannot use a PO box to register a business. You cannot manage your mail digitally with 24/7 access from anywhere.

## How does a Virtual Office plan work?

When you select a virtual office plan, you will be prompted to choose a local or toll-free phone and fax number after you log in to your personal Digital Mailbox. You can receive incoming calls to this virtual number and the call will automatically be forwarded to the phone number of your choice. You can receive and review fax conveniently from within your account. Your forwarding number can easily be changed at any time. You'll have an option to customize how many times the phone will ring before being forwarded to your voicemail. You can set your own voice message or type in the wording for a professional automated message. You'll receive a notification when a voicemail is received. You can easily listen to your voice messages from the iPostal1 app or your iPostal1 online mailbox. Outgoing fax is not a supported feature at this time. When you receive a call to your virtual phone number, the Caller ID will display your virtual phone number. This helps you to easily recognize these calls. We suggest saving your virtual phone number as a contact to allow you to quickly identify the source of the call.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## What is included in a Virtual Office plan and how does it work

When choosing a virtual office plan, you will receive a mailing address for your business, along with all the features of our Digital Mailbox service. What makes our Virtual Office plans different, is that you also get a phone line with call forwarding and voicemail capabilities, so you can have a business number linked to your mailing address and avoid using your personal phone for business. If you sign up for our Virtual Office plan, you receive: Virtual mailing address. Phone forwarding. Voice mail messaging with personal greeting. A dedicated electronic fax placed into your digital mailbox as a PDF.

## Can I Change my Plan?

You may change your monthly plan at any time, effective the next billing period. However, you may not change from a yearly plan to a monthly plan until the yearly billing period ends. Monthly plans can be upgraded to any other plan, including a yearly plan. Yearly plans can be upgraded to another yearly plan that allows for more mail items per month.

We keep your monthly cost low by charging for additional services only when you request them, this way you only pay for what you use. You may request a scan of the inside contents for any mail item for a small additional fee.

Prices are set by your mail center. iPostal1 displays real-time shipping rates for Purolator, based on your selected service level (e.g., overnight, 2-day, etc.). You can choose the option that best fits your budget and delivery timeline. Note: You can consolidate mail items into one package to save on shipping.

## Do you automatically open and scan my mail?

Mail is kept secure and confidential, when items arrive you will be notified via email or push notifications via our free iPostal1 App. We open your mail only if you specifically request us to scan the contents. We open packages only when you request us to take a picture of package content, or in order to ensure compliance with shipping regulations. Note: You can choose the auto-scan feature in which all letters that are received to your account are automatically requested for a content scan. This additional feature is only for letters and does not include boxes and packages.

## Can Someone else pick up my mail?

For security reasons, only the account holder can pick up mail at this time.

## Can I use my iPostal1 Mailing Address to receive Google Pin Codes?

Our addresses are not guaranteed to work for registrations with Google, Amazon, or Dun & Bradstreet. In most cases, these companies require address verification methods that our locations do not support. Additionally, Staples mail centers do not participate in Google Pin Code services or Amazon Business Registration and cannot scan or verify those postcards. If you choose to sign up and the address does not meet your needs, you may cancel within 30 days for a full refund.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## My mail arrived to my location but I don't see it in my account yet.

Many of our mail center locations upload mail once per day and may wait until a certain time of day to upload all mail items. If you received a delivery confirmation that your mail item was delivered from the carrier, your mail center may not have had the opportunity to upload items for the day. To avoid delays in receiving mail items: Your account must be fully active. All mail should include your full name or business name and full address including your mailbox number. Note: If you received a delivery notification from the carrier, we recommend contacting your mail center directly via phone to see if they can expedite uploading the item to your account.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## What should I do about Junk mail?

Most mail center locations will carefully sort out and recycle or discard all junk mail, such as flyers, circulars, advertising, and catalogs that are classified by Canada Post. When junk mail is discarded, it does not count toward your items per month received. If you receive any unsolicited junk mail that is uploaded to your account, you may choose to discard it at no additional charge.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## When will I receive the shipment I requested? (needs confirmation)

Shipments are sent based on the timeline that you choose and your destination address. You will only receive a tracking number, if you select a trackable shipping method. You tracking number will usually include a delivery date. For more information on the status of your shipping or consolidate and ship, please contact your location directly via phone. Note: Tracking is not included for USPS single letters 1-10 days and USPS First Class Mail. If you are shipping time sensitive or important mail, we recommend choosing a trackable shipping me thod.

Mail centers upload mail once per day, so a delay in uploading can occur.

## How does Consolidate and Ship work?

The "Consolidate and Ship" option lets your mail center combine multiple mail items into a single package and ship it to your specified destinationâ€”all in one simple step. Youâ€™ll choose your preferred shipping service level, and your mail will be sent as a consolidated shipment, saving both time and cost. Instead of submitting separate shipping requests for each item, this feature streamlines the process with a single request. Note: While you can select your preferred service level, pricing is not provided upfront. The final cost will be determined after the consolidated package is weighed.

## Who is listed as the sender of a forwarded package?

## Can I consolidate letters or packages before forwarding?

## What is a Mail Item?

A mail item is anything that arrives in your iPostal1 mailbox: any letter, package, or large envelope is one mail item.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Do you open my mail?

All your mail is kept secure and confidential, your mail center will only open your mail when you specifically request a scan, box image or a shipping task. Your mail center will open your mail when: You request a scan, your mail center will open the letter and scan the inside contents. You request a box image, your mail center will open your package and take images of the inside contents. You request to ship a package, your mail center may open your package in order to ensure compliance with shipping regulations.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## I received mail that is not addressed to me

When you pick up your mail at your mail center, you will be asked for ID and asked to sign for your mail items.

## My inbox says I have mail but I picked up all my mail

To ensure all mail is accounted for and to avoid storage fees, we recommend scheduling a pick up before picking up your mail items. When picking up up your mail at your mail center, you will be asked for ID and will be asked to sign for your mail items. Note: If you have mail in your inbox that you have already picked up, please contact your mail center via phone so that your pick up request can be processed.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## I havenâ€™t received any mail since signing up?

To ensure you start receiving mail to your mail center address you must complete the verification process. If you have already received a delivery confirmation from the carrier but don't see the mail in your account, it could be due to a delay in uploading the mail items by your mail center. Mail centers insert mail once per day, please allow time for your mail center to upload your mail. Note: Please be sure to provide your contacts the correct address, including your mailbox number. If your mailbox number is not included, your mail may be returned to the sender.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## How do I pay my Subscription and when is it due?

Your subscription payment is automatically billed using the primary credit card on file. You are billed each month or year, on the same day you signed up and depending on the plan you selected. To view and change the card on file: 1. Click on the drop down located on the right of the top toolbar, next to your U sername . Click on "Account Settings " . 2. Click "Payment Method" . To view your payment renewal date: 1. Click on "Mailbox Setting" located on the left toolbar. 2. Locate your payment renewal date under "General Settings" .

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## If I am behind on payments, how do I pay?

If you owe a balance, you will notice an alert with the total amount due, when logged in to your online account. You can simply update your payment method and pay your outstanding balance by following the prompts on your screen. Step 1. Click "Update Payment Method" to update your payment method. Step 2. Click "Continue to Payment" to make a payment. Step 3. You will see your current payment method, click "Pay Outstanding Balance" to pay.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## My credit card is not going through, what should I do?

Our system will automatically process your credit card in real-time. If you have attempted to enter your credit card details and it is not being accepted by the system please enter a different credit card. If your payment is being denied or declined, please contact your bank or financial institution.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Why do I need a credit card and what if I don't have one?

We require a valid payment method or an active credit card to be listed on your account in order to keep your account active. We will charge you each calendar month or year based on the plan you selected and the date you signed up. Any applicable taxes will also be included in that amount. Without a credit card or valid payment method on file, your account will not be activated for use.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## How are yearly plans charged?

Yearly plans renew only once a year. When you subscribe annually, youâ€™ll pay for ten months and receive two months free. This discount is included in the total price you pay. Example: Yearly Green Plan 30 = CA$ 149.00 per year. Monthly Green Plan 30 starts at CA$14.99 per month = $119.88 per year. Note: Our $99 annual subscription plan saves you two months on subscription fees.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click on "Transactions" , located in the drop down next to your username on the top right. 3. Click "View Details" to view past payments. You can download or p rint. Click on â€œTransaction Reportâ€ to view all transactions.

## Why do I have to pay to pick up my Mail?

Since digital mailboxes are not self-service like physical mailboxes, some mail centers charge a nominal fee for processing and retrieving your mail when you come in to pick it up. Pick up fees are charged, depending on the mail item type. Note: You can view your locationâ€™s pickup fees by navigating to the left-hand menu under "Services and Prices" in your web browser.

## Included features

Your inbox has many features that are automatically included at no additional cost: Real physical street address. Flexible shipment scheduling. (on request, weekly, bi-weekly, monthly) Personal Digital Mailbox - access online or with an app to manage mail. Your choice of ship dates and service level. Free App for Android and iPhone. Shipping to unlimited addresses, 24/7 digital access to all your mail items, unlimited secure cloud storage for scans and voice messages. 30 day storage: all mail & letterpacks; packages under 1,728 cu inches (= 12x12x12 size package) See a picture of the outside of every mail item. 10 day storage: packages 1,728 to 4,895 cu inches. Sender information for every item clearly visible. 5 day storage: packages at/over 4,896 cu inches (= 24x17x12 size package) Automatic email alert for new items received. Discard mail items service. Preparation of commercial invoice. (for international shipments) Consolidation of letters into one package for forwarding.

## Pickup price

A small fee will be charged when you pick up packages from your mail center. Pickup fees are due at the time of picking up your mail and it is charged to the payment method on file for your account. Pickup prices: Letters- Free to pick any amount of letters Letter packs- CAD1.50 per letter pack Packages- CAD1.50 per package To view your locations pickup pricing: 1. Go to iPostal.com . 2. Click on â€œLocationsâ€ , at the top of the screen. 3. Locate your mailing address. 4. Click "Click for More Details" , just below to show the exact pickup price for your mail center.

## Shipping and Consolidation

We offer comprehensive shipping services. When you log in to your account and choose to ship your mail, you'll be able to select the service level and pricing that best suit your needs Shipping Prices: Our system will provide an estimated shipping quote based on your mail center, the carrier and speed of shipping. Quotes are calculated by the weight and dimensions of the package and by the destination to where the item is being shipped. Additional fees may be applied to the quote/ regular shipping charges such as for labor and materials. Consolidation Prices: No charge for any number of letters consolidated. CA $2.95 per package or letter-pack consolidated. $1.95 for any number of magazines consolidated. Additional charge for packaging materials may be applied. Note: If you are shipping multiple items of various sizes together, we recommend you use the Consolidate feature, which will provide you a quote before shipping your mail items. When choosing "Consolidate and Ship", you will not see an estimated price until after your mail center weighs all of the mail items and processes the request. To view a quoted price, we recommend choosing a consolidation of mail first.

## Scanning and Shredding

Photos of the outside of your mail items are included with your plan. If you would like to view the inside contents of your mail item, you must request a scan for each item. An additional fee is charged per scan request. Discarding a mail item is usually free of charge, if you would like to shred the mail item instead, a fee is charged for each shredding request. The fee for a single scan or shred: CA $2.99 per letter, up to 10 pages, and an additional $0.25 per additional page.

## How often do I get charged for storage?

Storage fees are charged after the initial free storage period for a mail item has expired, each mail item has its own expiration date. To avoid storage fees, it is important to select an action for your mail items such as discard, shred, shipping or pickup. If no action is taken and the free storage period has expired, a storage fee is charged based on the mail item type. Note: The larger the mail item, the less amount of storage time is given, as it is taking up more space at your mail center location. Free storage period: â— Letters, large Envelopes, Magazines and Postcards: 30 FREE days. â— Small package: 10 FREE days. â— Large packages: 5 FREE days.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## I picked up my mail, why did I get storage fees?

To prevent unnecessary storage fees, please schedule a pickup in advance of picking up your mail. Your mail center will process the pickup at the time of you picking up. If the mail items were not updated when you picked up your mail, and it is still showing in your inbox, your account will continue to generate storage fees. Note: If you would like to request a retroactive storage refund, please contact us directly. All storage refunds need to be approved by your mail center before processing.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## When was I informed of storage fees?

An email notification is sent to you 3 days in advance, before the mail item expires, notifying you that a storage fee will be incurred soon, if no action is taken for the mail items. This allows you time to take action on your mail items by: Shipping, Picking up, Discarding or Shredding. Expiration date: You can view the expiration date for each mail item, when signed in to your account. The expiration date is located towards the center of the page and to the right of the mail item image.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## How long can I hold mail or packages in my mailbox?

You receive 30 days free storage for all letters, magazines and letter packs. Packages are given 5 - 10 days, depending on the size. Once your expiration date is expired, you will begin to be charged storage. Letters and flat mail are charged CA $1.79 /item per month. Packages that exceed 28,316.74 cubic centimeters (equivalent to 30.48 cm Ã— 30.48 cm Ã— 30.48 cm) are given 10 days free storage. Packages that exceed 80,217.55 cubic centimeters (equivalent to 60.96 cm Ã— 43.18 cm Ã— 30.48 cm) are given 5 days free storage. Note: Packages are charged CA $1.79/pound* per every 5, 10, or 30 days - According to the size and storage time frame allotted to the package. *Greater of actual weight or dimensional weight. To avoid storage charges, recycle, shred, forward, or pick up mail items within your free storage period. Once the free storage period has exceeded, all storage fees will be applied automatically. You do not have to do anything extra in your account.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## How to request a refund

If you qualify and would like to request a refund, please contact customer support directly and an agent will be happy to assist you. All refunds must be approved before processing. Subscription: If your account has been cancelled within the first 30 days and has been unused, you are eligible to request a refund. Other Refunds: Storage, Shipping and other service refunds will need to be approved by your mail center location before we can proceed with processing the refund.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Can the rest of my annual subscription be refunded?

If you have an annual subscription and choose to cancel within 30 days, youâ€™re eligible for a full refund. To request the refund, please contact iPostal1 customer support directly.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## When will I receive my refund?

If you qualify for a refund for your subscription fees and you have already requested a refund with a customer support agent, it will generally take 3-5 business days to process. All other refunds including storage or shipping refunds, will need to be approved first by your mail center, before processing and can take longer at times.
