## How to Schedule a Pick Up

You can pick up your mail in person at your mail center address by requesting a Scheduled Pick Up from inside your inbox. Scheduling a pick-up will ensure that your mail will be updated when you arrive which prevents unnecessary storage charges. Your mail center will ask for ID when picking up mail and a small fee may be charged to pick up. You can find your locations pick up hours directly in your mailbox and If you may have any questions, please contact your mail center directly. To Schedule a Pick Up: Step 1. Select the mail item(s) from inside your inbox and click on the "Schedule Pickup" button from the top toolbar. Step 2. Select an available pickup date by clicking on the calendar date , then you can proceed to choose a time for your scheduled pick-up. Step 3. To finish, scroll down and click the "Schedule " button to complete your request. Your mail center will receive an alert that you are coming in to pick up your mail on the date and time selected. When you arrive, you will be asked to sign for your mail items and you will be charged the pickup fee.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## How to request a shipment for a single mail item?

Creating a shipping request can easily send or forward your mail to your home address. After you have submitted your shipping request, your mail center will receive an alert to process. Once the request is completed, you will receive an email confirmation with the order details and tracking number, if you selected a trackable shipping method. Note: All shipping labels are generated at your mail center, private or personal labels are not allowed for shipping. How to create a shipping request on a desktop or mobile browser: Step 1. Login to the iPostal1 website. Select the item you would like to ship and click on the "Ship" button on the top toolbar. The "Ship" option is only available for one item. If you are shipping multiple items, you can choose "Consolidate & Ship" , and all of the mail will become one item with a new a weight and dimensions. Step 2. Select a Shipping Address where you would like to have your mail shipped to. If the address is displayed in the center dropdown, Click the "Continue" button located at the bottom right of the page. You can add a new address by clicking on "+Add a New Address" . Fill in the required information and click on "Add Shipping Address" when finished. Step 3. Fill in the required information and enter any special instructions at the bottom of the page (if applicable) and click "Continue" when finished. Step 4. Select your shipping method. The mail will be sent out with the service level of your choice. Click "Continue" when finished. Step 5. Verify that all your information is correct, and click "Ship" when finished. Please allow 24 - 48hrs for all requests to be processed. For shipping request status, please contact your mail center directly via phone.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## How to ship multiple mail items at once?

Save time and request a "Consolidate and Ship" for all of your mail items at once. Your mail center will combine the selected mail items together and ship according to your selected options. When you choose this option, you will not see any shipping rates or prices. When consolidating and shipping in one step, a price quote is not provided. If you would like to view a price for shipping, please request a "Consolidation" first. To ship multiple mail items at once: Step 1. Login to your account and select all of the mail items you would like to ship together, and choose the "Consolidate & Ship" button on the top toolbar. Step 2. Select a shipping address from the drop down menu. You can also click the "Add a New address" button, if needed. Step 3. Select Optional Services or enter Special Instructions, if needed. Step 4. Choose your shipping method and click the "Continue" button. The mail item will be shipped with the service level that you select. The price will depend on the shipping speed, and the weight and dimensions of the combined letters or package . Step 5. Please verify that all your information is correct and click the "Ship" button. Step 6. Your Mail Center will get an alert to process your request. Please allow 24 - 48 hrs for your request to be processed by your mail center. You will receive an email confirmation when your mail has been shipped. A tracking number will be included in your confirmation order, only if you have chosen a trackable shipping method. If you would like a quote in advance of shipping, please select a "Consolidation" of mail first. After your consolidation is complete, you can log into your account and request a shipment for your consolidated mail item. You will then see a quoted price for shipping. Note: The new consolidated mail item ID will begin with the letter "C".

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## How to get a shipping quote for multiple mail items or packages?

To receive a shipping quote for shipping multiple mail items together, you can request a consolidation of mail. Your mail center location will combine all the selected mail items into one package. You will receive an alert when it is completed, so you can log in and choose your desired shipping option with the correct pricing. If you are shipping packages internationally, please ensure that you have notarized your documents using the online notary. How to Consolidate multiple mail items: Step 1. Login to your account and select two or more mail items, then click on the '' Consolidate" Button in the top toolbar. Step 2. Enter special instructions for your mail center in the text box. Then click the "Consolidate" button. The cost for consolidation is $1.95 per package, letters and postcards are free to consolidate. Your mail center will receive an alert to process your request and send you an email confirmation when completed. Note: The new consolidated mail item ID will begin with the letter "C". After your consolidation is complete, you can log into your account and request a shipment for your consolidated mail item. You will then see a quoted price for shipping.

## How to discard mail I don't want

We understand that you may receive items in your inbox that you don't need. You can choose to discard mail items free of charge. Your mail center will dispose of the unwanted mail items you include in your request and the mail item will be deleted from your inbox. If your mail items are important, we recommend you choose the mail Shredding option instead. Step 1 . To discard mail, start by selecting the mail item(s) you wish to discard from your inbox. Then, click on the "Discard" button in the top toolbar. Step 2. Click " Continue" to submit your request. Your Mail Center will get an alert to process your request and you will receive an email confirmation when it is completed. For discard request status, please contact your mail center directly via phone. Note: When you request to discard mail, the item will be placed in regular or recycling trash. Once the mail item is discarded, any associated images or scans will be permanently deleted from our system.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## How to request a scan of the inside contents of your mail item?

You can request a scan to view the inside contents of your letter. When selecting to scan, your mail center will open the envelope and scan the images. After the task is completed, the images will be in your inbox for you to view. The charge for a scan of the inside contents is CA $2.99 for the first 10 pages of each letter and $.25 each additional page. Credit Cards and Gift Cards cannot be scanned. Step 1. To scan the inside contents of your mail, please login to your account, select the mail item that you would like to be scanned and click on the "Scan" button in the toolbar above. Step 2. Choose an option for what you want to do with the mail after the scan has been completed. Scan and Put Back in My Mailbox: Original mail will be saved until you choose to Ship, Pickup, Shred or Discard. Scan and Discard: Scan will be saved in your inbox, and original mail will be discarded. Scan and Shred: Scan will be saved in your inbox, and original mail will be shredded. Please note that shredding cannot be reversed once it is completed and a small fee is added for the shredding request. Step 3. Scroll down and click on "Scan" to submit your request. The status of your mail item will be updated to "Scan Requested" in your inbox immediately after you submit your request. If you have already requested a Scan, please allow 24 - 48hrs for your mail center to process. If you need an update on the status of your request, please contact your mail center directly via phone. When your order has been fulfilled, the status will read "Scanned". Your completed scan will be viewable as a PDF in your inbox. You can download your PDF, or forward it as an attachment. If your scanned images are not visible, missing a page or you may have an issue with the quality of the scan, please contact support. Please be sure to save any scans. The scanned images are deleted from our system once you select an action, such as: discard, ship, pick up, shred etc. You will no longer be able to view these in your inbox.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## How to shred mail items

You can choose to shred a mail item and your mail center will open the letter and shred the inside contents of the letter. The fee to shred is CA $2.99 per letter. This includes up to 10 pages and CA $.25 for each additional page. Discounted Scan/Shred Bundles can be purchased by clicking on the underlined link above your top toolbar. Step 1. To shred mail, please select the mail item you wish to shred from your inbox and then click the "Shred" button located in the top toolbar. Step 2. Click "Continue" . Your Mail Center will receive an alert to process your request, and you will receive an email confirmation when it is completed. Please allow 24 - 48 hrs for all tasks to be processed. Note: Once mail is shredded, it is no longer available to view. To check the status of your Shred request please contact your mail center. If you need to cancel a shredding request, please contact your mail center immediately via phone.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## How to change my mail request on a desktop computer

If you would like to make a change or cancel your shipping, scan, discard, shred or pickup request, you can do so only if the request has not already been processed by your mail center. If you would like to make a change to a request, please cancel the request first and submit a new request. If your request is processing or no longer showing, please contact your mail center directly via phone. To change or cancel a mail request: Step 1. Please click the "Open Requests" Button to view all your requests. Step 2. Click "Cancel Request" on each item you wish to cancel. Step 3. Click "Yes" or "No" to continue. Note: If you do not see a status, please contact your mail center directly via phone, as they may have already started processing your request.

## How to Enable or Disable Automatic Scan

The Auto-scan feature will automatically scan all mail items received in your Inbox upon arrival. The charge for scanning the inside contents of mail will apply when this feature is enabled. Scroll down the bottom of the "Notifications" box. Step 3. To turn On: click the toggle from "Off" to "On" . To turn Off: click the toggle from "On" to "Off" . Step 4. Autoscan is now enabled/ disabled.

## How to Enable Automatic Shipping

The Autoship feature lets you choose how often all your mail is automatically shipped to the address you have on file. Once a mail item is received at your mail center, it can be shipped according to your selection. Each shipment will be charged based on the shipping rates at your location. Note: The default setting is "No Autoship". To enable the Autoship feature: Step 1. Click on "Mailbox Settings" located in the left toolbar. Step 2. Choose an Autoship frequency by clicking on the dropdown menu located under "Autoship Options" and make your selection (Weekly/Every Two Weeks/Monthly). Step 3. Scroll down to the " Autoship Options" box and click on the dropdown menus below to select your desired International/Domestic Carrier settings. You will need to make a selection for both International and Domestic, even if you are only shipping domestic. Please select the day of the week you would like your items shipped and whether or not you would like to be notified each time a shipment is prepared. Step 4. Select if you would like to receive a notification when your shipment is prepared. Note: Your mail center will automatically receive ship your mail according to the setting you selected.

## Can I pause my iPostal1 Subscription?

The "On Hold" feature allows approved accounts to place their mailbox on hold for a duration of three, six, or twelve months for a one-time fee. This feature applies to customers who have been active for three or more months and have yet to come off a hold within the last three months. You will retain the mailbox number and address throughout the hold period. Note: Please be sure to empty your Inbox by discarding, shipping, or scheduling a Pick Up for your mail items, and pay any outstanding balance; otherwise, the hold feature will not be available. To place an account On Hold: Step 1. Log in to your account and click "Mailbox Settings" in the left hand toolbar. Step 2. Click "Cancel Mailbox". Step 3. Choose from the three options of 3 Months, 6 Months, or 12 Months by clicking the "Select" button. Step 4. Choose your payment method and click "Confirm".

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## How to cancel my account using a desktop

You can cancel your account at any time by logging into your account on a mobile browser or desktop. Before canceling your mailbox, please empty your inbox by discarding, shipping, or shredding your mail items. Please ensure you have made copies of all uploaded documents, as they will be deleted when your account is canceled. If you would like to re-activate your account, your number will be saved for 90 days. Once your account is closed, mail will no longer be accepted at your location. Please remember to update your contacts with your new mailing address. If you are not able to click the cancel button, please verify that you have cleared all of the mail items in your inbox and are up to date with your payment. To cancel your account using a desktop browser: Step 1. Click on "Mailbox Settings" , located in the left toolbar. Step 2. Scroll down to the bottom of the Mailbox Setting box and click the "Cancel Mailbox" button. Step 3. To finalize the cancellation of your iPostal1 Digital Mailbox, click "Yes" . You will then receive an email confirmation that your account has been canceled. You will no longer be charged for your subscription. Note: If you don't see this option, please take action on your mail items by selecting a discard, shipping or shred. After your mailbox is empty, come back to this page, and the Cancel Mailbox button will be active.

## How to upgrade or downgrade your plan

You can easily upgrade or downgrade your plan directly in your account. When upgrading, you will be prompted to pay the difference of the plan selected, if applicable. Step 1. Login to your iPostal1 account. Click the "Mailbox Settings" located in the left toolbar. Step 2. Click the "Change Plan" button located under general settings. Step 3. Scroll down to see all your options and click on the plan that's right for you. Step 4. Review your plan and click "Place Order" . Your primary credit card on file will be charged the updated rate for your new subscription.

If you are selecting a Mail Center in the US, select the State and City of the address that you would like to add. Step 3. Select the Address that you prefer an r eview the locations details and pricing. Plan pricing for each location will be displayed at the bottom of your screen and may be different at each address. Step 4. Choose the plan that's right for you. Step 5. Confirm your email address and phone number. Agree to terms and c lick "Add Location" and y our new mailbox will be purchased with the primary credit card on file. Step 6. Click on: "Go To My Mailbox" to receive an email confirmation to complete the verification process. If you choose a US location, you will be charged in USD and a notarized USPS form 1583 will be required. Click: "Start" to begin. Step 7. Once your new address has been purchased, you can switch between your addresses by clicking the dropdown arrow, located next to your address. Note : To add a new iPostal1 location or mailbox account, you must have a valid payment method on file. Verification processes may vary depending on the location you choose. When opening an account at any U.S. location, a USPS Form 1583 must be notarized through our online notary service.

## How to ship mail using the iPostal1 App

Shipping your mail is simple via the iPostal1 App. To begin, login to the iPostal1 App using your username and password. Shipping one single mail item: you can select the mail item, and click on "Ship" . Shipping more than one item: you will need to consolidate the mail first, in order for shipping options to show. Shipping multiple mail items together in one step: c hoose a " Consolidate and Ship " instead. How to create a shipping request in the iPostal1 App: Step 1. Select the mail item that you wish to ship by tapping on the green icon to the left of your mail item number. A menu will appear immediately on the right side of your screen. Then tap "Ship" . Step 2. Select the address where you wish to ship the mail item(s) and and tap "Next" . Step 3. Enter any special Instructions and tap "Next" . Step 4. Choose your preferred shipping method and tap "Next" . Step 5. Verify that your information is accurate and tap "Send Request" to complete your order. Your mail center will automatically receive your request and will ship your mail soon. The status in your Inbox will be updated to "Ship Requested" . Note: After your request has been processed, the item will be removed from your inbox. You can confirm that the request was completed by checking your mail history.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## How to scan mail items in the iPostal1 App

You can request a scan of the inside contents of your mail items and view the images, conveniently from the iPostal1 App. Note: Credit Cards, Gift Cards and select items that contain private information cannot be scanned. To scan a mail item in your iPostal1 App: Step 1. Log into your account in the iPostal1 App, using your username and password. Step 2. Select the items of mail that you wish to scan by tapping on the green icon, located to the left of the mail item number. Then tap "Scan" in the Inbox Menu. Or you can tap on the mail item itself and then tap on the taskbar menu, located in the top right corner. Step 3. Select a scan option and tap "Send Request" , located at the bottom right corner. Step 4. The status of your mail item will now read "Scan Requested" . After your mail center has proc essed your order, the status will be updated to "Scanned" . After your mail center has processed your order, the status will be updated to "Scanned". To View the scanned item, tap on the mail item in your inbox and then tap on the image.

## How to consolidate to get a shipping quote in the iPostal1 App

You can choose to consolidate several mail items at once. After your consolidation request has been processed, your mail items will be combined into one package and you will then be able to view a shipping quote. To consolidate your mail items in the iPostal1 App: Step 1. Log into your account in the iPostal1 App, using your username and password. Step 2. Select the items of mail that you wish to consolidate by tapping on the green icon to the left of the shipping number. Then tap on "Consolidate" in the Inbox Menu. Step 3. Confirm your order by tapping "Send Request". Step 4. The status for the mail items will change to "Consolidate Requested". After your mail center has processed your order, the status will be updated to "Consolidated". Both mail items will now appear together in one new package. The mail item number will begin with the letter C. Once your new consolidated mail item appears in your inbox, select the mail item starting with a "C" to begin a shipping task. You will then see real-time shipping rates for that mail item.

## How to set up Automatic Shipping in the iPostal1 App

The Auto ship feature will automatically ship any mail you receive based on frequency you select. You are charged per shipment, based on the mail item dimensions and speed you choose. To set up automatic shipping in the iPostal1 App: Step 1. Log on to your iPostal1 App using your username and password. Step 2. Tap on the "Menu" icon, located in the top left corner. Step 3. Tap on "Account Settings". Step 4. Tap on "Mailbox Configuration". Step 5. Select your shipping frequency based on the options provided: upon request, weekly, every two weeks or monthly. If you select "Upon Request", autoship will not be activated. You will be required to login each time you would like to create a shipment. Step 6. Choose your preferred "Domestic Shipping Level". Step 7. Tap "Done". *You can log back into your account to change your shipping settings at any time.

To finish, the system will ask you to confirm that this is what you would like to do. Note: If you cancel your account by mistake, please reach out to customer support for assistance.

## Technical issues on the website

If you are experiencing technical issues with our website, such as invalid token or server error please try the following steps: 1. Clear Browser Cache and Cookies: Sometimes, old cookies and cached data can cause issues with website functionality. 2. Use another browser: Using another browser such as google, chrome, safari, edge or incognito/private browsing mode can help bypass some browser-related issues. 3. Check Browser Settings: Ensure that your browser is set to accept cookies and that there are no extensions blocking the website's functionality. 4. Update Browser: Make sure your browser is up-to-date to avoid compatibility issues. 5. Contact Support: If the issue persists, it may be helpful to contact our support team for further assistance.

## How to sign up

Signing up is easy, y ou can sign up directly through our website by clicking "Sign Up", located at the top right of your screen and follow the instructions to create an account . If you a choosing a location is Canada, please contact customer support for more details on the requirements and verification process. Note: For verification purposes you must create the account under your legal name and address listed on your IDs. If you are using this for business purposes, you can add your business name to your account at signup. Upon signup, you will be required to submit a notarized USPS Form 1583, along with 2 acceptable IDs. Once that has been received and approved by your mail center, youâ€™ll have full access to your account and the mail that arrives to your new virtual mailing address. Step 1. Choose a Location and Plan . C hoose a physical address from 4,000 + digital mailbox locations across the U.S. and abroad, this address will be where you will receive your mail. To view a list of all of our address locations please visit our locations page, click on Locations at the top of our site, then choose the state and city or or click here . Then select the plan that is best for you, depending on how much mail you expect to receive. Step 2. Checkout Provide your contact information and select a payment method via a credit card or PayPal account. Step 3. Form 1583 or Verification Process. Form 1583 for U.S. locations After signing up, you will be assigned a personal mailbox number and a USPS Form 1583 that authorizes your digital mailbox location to receive mail on your behalf. You will need two forms of acceptable IDs and you can then choose to notarize online or in person at your mail center location. To notarize online, please select online notary and follow the link that is sent to your email. If you will visiting your mail center to notarize in person, please call ahead to be sure that they offer on site notary. iPostal1 makes this process easy. or Verification process for all locations outside of the U.S. The verification process for locations outside of the U.S. may differ. Please contact customer support for more information. Step 4. Redirect Your Mail after your account is fully approved. To begin receiving mail at your new address, file a Temporary Change of Address form with the USPS and/or notify senders directly, once your account is approved. With your new virtual mailing address, you will be able to: View and manage your mail from anywhere 24/7. See your mail as soon as it is received. Use our free app or any computer to view an image of the outside of each mail item you receive. With a click or tap, tell your mail center what you want to do with each item: forward, scan, schedule a pickup, discard, or shred. Receive Mail & Packages from Any Carrier. Because every iPostal1 digital mailbox address is a real street address, not a standard postal box, you can receive mail and packages not only from the USPS, but also from FedEx, UPS and other carriers. Add Locations with Just a Click. It's fast and easy to add additional address locations for business or personal use. Manage mail for all locations from one login. Note: If the address you are choosing is located in Canada, please contact customer support for details on the requirements.

## Requirements

To open a virtual iPostal1 mailbox, you will be required to provide the following: Valid payment method: W e accept American Express, Visa, MasterCard, and Discover and PayPal. U.S. locations: If your mailbox is located in the US, a completed form 1583 that is notarized online or completed at your mail center. Locations outside of the U.S.: Please contact customer support for more details. Identification: 2 acceptable IDs from the list; 1 photo ID and 1 address ID (must match the name used to sign up). Address: A current address that matches your photo ID. To notarize online: A mobile phone or computer with strong internet connection and access to video and microphone. Note: If you are unable to add your address or your country is not listed as an option, please contact customer support for assistance. If you don't have a U.S. address you must still file the USPS form 1583. You'll be required to notarize the Form 1583 using our online notary service for $25. If your mailbox location is in Canada, the requirements may be different. Please contact customer support for more details.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Select your plan

iPostal1 offers Virtual Mailing Address plans for personal use only starting at $9.99/month, and Virtual Business Address plans to receive mail under a business name as well as for personal use, starting at $14.99/month. Each plan has four options, depending on how much mail you expect to receive each month. We offer Virtual Office plans that may be used with a business name and for personal use, and come with phone forwarding and fax, starting at $39.99/month. Get two months free on any plan when you select a Yearly plan. You may change your monthly plan at any time, effective the next billing period. Note: Yearly plans can be upgraded to another yearly plan that allows you to receive more mail items per month. However, you may not change from a yearly plan to a monthly plan until the yearly billing period ends. Most of our locations are Standard addresses that start at $9.99/month. Addresses in prestigious buildings or in locations where costs and demand are higher, may cost more according to the address type: Select +$10; Premium +$20; Prestige +$30.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

C hoose a physical address from 4,000 + digital mailbox locations across the U.S. and abroad, this address will be where you will receive your mail. ## Adding additional mail recipients to your account at sign up

You can add up to 6 recipients to a personal account or up to 5 additional recipients and 1 business name to a business account. Some locations in Canada are limited to 1 recipient at this time, please contact customer support for more details. For U.S. locations: To add an additional recipient such as your spouse, child, employee at the same time as the primary recipient during the signup process, use the Form Assistant, located in your digital mailbox account, to guide you through completing the form. After completing the steps, youâ€™ll receive two separate Forms to notarize and submit, along with copies of two forms of ID for each individual. Please contact support if you would like to arrange a joint session to notarize online. Once you have completed the notary session, please contact support for assistance with adding the notarized documents to the account. Adult children (age 18 and older) must provide their own signed and notarized Form 1583 and 2 forms of ID. Spouses also require their own form per new regulations. For locations outside of the U.S.: Please contact customer support for assistance. Note: To add or remove additional recipients after your account is approved, please contact customer support directly.

## Adding a business name when signing up

You can add your business name directly to your account through step 3 of the USPS 1583 form assistant located once you log into your account. Please be sure that you selected a business plan and not a personal plan. This will then be reflected in your account, as well as on line 9 of the 1583 form. Once your account is approved, we will be able to start receiving mail under your business name. If your account is already approved and you would like to add a business name, please upgrade to a business plan. Note: According to the USPS requirements, you can only have one business name per business account. If you have a second business, you can easily create a second account by clicking on "Add a Location" from your first digital mailbox account. You can even add a second mailbox at the same address. If you have entered the incorrect name at signup, you can edit your name by clicking on the yellow banner across the top of your account.

## Forwarding mail to your new iPostal1 address

A change of address is recommended when youâ€™d like your mail to be redirected to your new iPostal1 address. After your account is fully approved, we recommend completing the temporary change of address in person at a Post Office near you. We have found that the online change of address system, unfortunately, doesn't always recognize/accept the addresses because of the added suite number, so please complete this in person to avoid any issues or delays. Upon signup, we assign you a unique suite number to go along with the address you selected - this is to set you apart from the other customers signing up at the same location. For this reason, it is an important part of the address and is required to be listed on any incoming mail. Note: We recommend updating your address, after your account is fully approved by your mail center. We do not recommend filing a Permanent Change of Address form with the USPS. A Temporary Change of Address is good for 6 months and may be renewed for an additional 6 months.

## Closing an account within 30 days

If you choose to close your account within the first 30 days of opening, you may receive a refund of the mailbox rental fee if you did not use your account to receive mail or for any other purpose. Please contact iPostal1 to see if you qualify and to request a refund. Note: If you filed a Temporary Change of Address form with your Post Office, you can easily cancel the Temp address change, and file a new one. However, if you filed a Permanent Change of Address, you will need to inform your senders individually that your address has changed.

## What is a Form 1583 and why do I need one?

The USPS Form 1583 is a 'Permission Slip' that you sign to allow your mail to be processed by a third party address. This form is required if you choose a mail center address in the United States. Most people who sign up are new to the concept. We are happy to explain why you need one for your online mailbox. Providing your IDs, notary and signature verify that you are the one who authorizes mail to come to your account. We provide you with a pre-filled form 1583 inside of your account and easy access to an online notary. Your form 1583 is automatically uploaded to your account after the online notary session is completed. You can notarize directly at your mail center, if your location provides this service. Your location will upload your documents to your account. Please call ahead and be sure to have your required documents available when visiting your mail center. We do not accept local notaries, such as from a bank or any other personal notary. 1583 Forms cannot be notarized at the post office. Forms cannot not be uploaded or submitted via email or fax. Your mailbox location is classified by USPS as a Commercial Mail Receiving Agency (CMRA) and reports to the local Post Office. According to USPS law, in order for your Address Location to legally process mail on your behalf, the Form 1583 is required to be on file in the address location that you selected. They also will be uploading a copy of your form to the USPS database. Form 1583 must be properly signed by the mailbox renter and notarized using our online notary partner, Proof.com, or it can be signed at your mail center. Only after your mail center/ CMRA has properly reviewed the Form 1583 along with your two valid forms of ID. You will be able to begin receiving mail and request tasks for your mail, after your account is fully approved. Prior to this time, your mail and packages are subject to be returned to sender in accordance with USPS guidelines. Once your form 1583 is approved, your mail can start the journey to your iPostal1 Mailbox. Form 1583 does: Provide permission for mail to be received on behalf of the mailbox renter Verify the identity of the mailbox renter Require two acceptable IDs Require a notary or agent signature Form 1583 does not: Reroute mail from your home or business (This CAN be done through a separate 'Change of Address' Form at your local Post Office) Share/publicize your new address with the world - it is up to you to share your address with the people who send you Note: If your mailbox location is in Canada, the verification process may be different. Please contact customer support for more information.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Step by Step instructions for the Form 1583 assistant

To begin the form 1583 process, please sign into your account via a desktop computer. Once all of the information is filled out, your form 1583 will appear in your account. To arrange an online notary session, please select 'Continue with Online Notary' then follow the link that is sent to your email. You can then choose to notarize online via proof.com or you can visit your mail center to have your documents notarized, if in person notary service is available at your mail center. Local notaries, such as banks are not allowed. Please contact customer support directly if you are experiencing an issue with submitting your documents. Click "Learn More", located on the yellow banner at the top of your account. Click "Edit Form 1583 Information" . If you do not see the yellow banner on your account, click on the bell icon at the top right of your screen and cancel your online notary session. Step 1. Mail Recipients for this Account: Enter the legal name of the primary mail recipient. The name should match the name that appears on your government issued ID. If this is a business account that will receive mail for a company , please select "Yes" . You will be asked to enter your business information when you reach Step 3. If this is not a business account and you would like to add additional recipients, please select "Yes" . Enter the full legal name and last name of your spouse/significant other. You may also enter the full legal names (first and last required) of up to three minor children. Note: If a spouse is added on this step, both the primary recipient and their spouse will need to generate a Form 1583, provide ID's, and notarize online or at your mail center. If you wish to add an additional mail recipient that is not a spouse/significant other or minor child, you will need to have that additional recipient fill out and notarize their own Form 1583. You can request a joint online notary session for a discount, by contacting iPostal1 customer support. Step 2. Your Address - As listed on your government-issued ID: Enter your home address as it appears on your Address ID document. You will also be asked whether you'd like to hide your email address on the form, if you have a U.S. Social Security Number, and if you will be shipping items outside of the U.S. Step 3 - Your Business Information: Select whether this is a registered business. Then, enter the requested business information below. Step 4 - Mail Recipient Identification Documents: Select the type of photo ID that you will be providing your mail center. The Photo ID should be a valid, government-issued photo ID from the list of approved ID's. Then, select the type of address ID that you will be providing your mail center. Your address IDs must verify the home address you listed in Step 2 and be on the list of approved ID's. All ID's should be current, and not soon to expire. Step 5 - Review: Please verify that all the information listed on this page is correct. Step 6 - Notarize 1583 Option 1 - Online Notary: Proof.com, our online notary partner, is standing by for immediate processing. This option requires a webcam or smartphone. The cost for using proof.com is $25. Your notarized form and ID's will be automatically uploaded to your account with the online notary option. Please click on Continue with Online Notary to proceed. Option 2 - Mail Center Location: Some of our mail centers offer Notary services in house. If your location offers this service, you can notarize your form 1583 in person. If not, then you will have to notarize your 1583 through our online notary partner, Proof.com. Note: If you are signing up from an International address and/or if you would like to ship items outside of the U.S., you are required to notarize your USPS form 1583 using the online notary, proof.com.

## Which IDs can I provide for the USPS Form 1583?

Two forms of identification are required, a Primary Photo ID and a Secondary Proof of Address ID. Your 2 IDs are required to be submitted along with your form 1583. You can notarize online, using proof.com or you can visit your mail center location, if notary service is provided at your location. Please call ahead to see if notary service is provided. Only the IDs listed here are accepted by iPostal1. If you have any questions or need clarification, please contact customer support. Acceptable Photo IDs: Valid state-issued driverâ€˜s license Non-driverâ€™s identification card U.S. passport, U.S. passport card Foreign passport Matricula Consular card (Mexico) NEXUS card (Canada) Acceptable Proof of Address Documents: Current lease Mortgage or deed of trust Voter or vehicle registration card Home or vehicle insurance policy Unacceptable IDs: Social Security cards Credit cards Utility bills Birth certificates National ID Cards Bank Statements University Card U.S. Armed Forces card, Uniformed Service ID card U.S. certificate of citizenship or naturalization Identification card issued by a federally or state-recognized tribal nation (tribal identification card) Note: The Primary ID must have a clear photograph of the mail recipient. International customers must use their passport as their photo ID. We accept the international equivalent of the Secondary IDs listed. Leases must be current. We do not accept month to month leases. International leases require a Certified Translation.

## Where do I add my business name?

If you selected a business plan and entered a business name in step 3 when you signed up for your mailbox, our system will automatically place your business name in box 7 on the USPS form 1583. Box 7 is the correct box for your business name and is available when you select a business plan. For business account use, you may add a total of 1 business name and 5 personal names associated with one account. Note: Each additional recipient is required to provided 2 acceptable IDs and a notarized form 1583. Each additional business name or DBA requires its own separate account.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## If I am using my mailbox for business only, do I need my personal name on the 1583?

USPS requires every mailbox account with a business name, to have a personal name attached to the account for verification purposes. Even if all of your mail will only be addressed to the business name alone, your personal name, signature and IDs need to be on file. The business name will be listed in box 7. Mail can arrive addressed to the business name without your personal name. Note: We will not share your personal information with anyone. USPS requires that information to be on file, in order for us to legally receive mail for your account.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## How to add a spouse, minor child or additional person to my mailbox?

You can add up to 5 additional names with a personal mailbox for a total of 6 recipients names or 6 personal names and 1 business name for a business account. If your mailbox location is in the U.S., each additional recipient, will require their own notarized Form 1583 and will need to submit 2 valid forms of ID. If your mailbox location is outside of the U.S., please contact support, as the requirements may be different. Some locations in Canada are limited to 1 customer name at this time. Please be sure to list additional recipients such as a spouse, adult children, and any minor children who are being added to your account in step 1 of the form assistant. Since minors are not of age and do not have IDs, they are not required to file their own 1583. Some mail centers may ask for proof that a recipient is a minor. Adult children (age 18 and older) must provide their own signed and notarized Form 1583 and 2 forms of ID. Spouses and any other additional recipients over the age of 18 are also required their own form, per new regulations. To add or edit additional mail recipients to your account during sign up: Step 1. Navigate to step 1 and scroll towards the middle. Step 2. Click " Yes" under " Would you like to add additional mail recipient(s) to your account", then click " Next" . Note: If you already have an open account or do not see the form assistant, please contact customer support directly.

## Does the USPS form 1583 change my address?

The USPS form 1583 does not change your address, it simply gives your mail center permission to handle mail that arrives in your name. Once your account is fully approved by your mail center, you can update your contact and file a change of address. You will be required to fill out a separate temporary change of address form with USPS to change your address so that mail is forwarded. We recommend filling out a temporary change of Address , as any permanent change of address cannot be reverted in the future.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Can I enter my mailbox address as my business address on the form 1583?

Your business address should be the actual place you conduct your business at. If you do not have a business address, you can use your home address in this section of the form 1583.

## If I don't have a company, what should I write in the Form 1583?

A company name is not required to complete the Form 1583. If you did not sign up for a business plan and are not expecting mail for your business, you may leave the company information field blank on Form 1583.

## Do I have to provide my current address on the form 1583?

The USPS requires your current address to be listed on the Form 1583. You will also be required to provide 2 acceptable IDs. A current photo ID and a proof of address ID, that matches your current address entered when signing up.

If your mailbox location is outside of the U.S. the requirements and verification may be different. Please contact customer support for more details.

## Do I have to get the Form 1583 notarized?

The USPS requires notarization of Form 1583 to prevent identity fraud, protecting you and the mail center. Many mail centers allow you to provide your IDs and sign the form in person in their presence, where the staff can review your IDs and verify your identity. Some mail centers charge for this service, so please check with them about details. T o notarize your form without going to your mail center, you will be required to use our online notary service for $25. All customers living outside of the U.S. or are shipping outside of the U.S, are required to use our online notary service. Note: You cannot fill out your Form 1583 at the Post Office. Local notaries, such as banks, are not acceptable. Online Notary is required: If you live outside of the U.S. If you have international documents. If you are shipping to an international location. If you have U.S. documents but cannot visit your mail center in person to provide your IDs and sign the form 1583. If your mail center does not allow you to sign the form in person. Online Notary is not required: If you visit your mail center location, provide your acceptable U.S. IDs and sign the form 1583 in person.

## Why is my only option the online notary?

## How do I submit the 1583 Form and ID to you?

## Is my account approved after notarizing my documents online?

Submitting your required documents and completing the online notary session is the first step but does not confirm that your account is approved. Once these completed documents are submitted, they are reviewed by our team and sent to your mail center location for final approval. You can verify the approval status of your account in the following ways: 1. Email Notification: You should have received an email from your Mail Center notifying you that your USPS Form 1583 has been approved. 2. Account Dashboard: The yellow box inside your account, containing Form 1583 instructions, will disappear from your screen once your account is approved. 3. Mailbox Settings: You can log into your account, click on "Mailbox Settings" located on the left toolbar, and check "General Settings" to see if your mailbox address is active and approved. If you have followed these steps and still have doubts about your account approval, I recommend reaching out to customer support for further assistance.

## I already notarized my form 1583

If you have already notarized a document using a local notary, it will not be accepted for upload. If you live in the U.S. and have U.S. documents: many mail centers will allow you to bring your IDs and Form 1583 to sign in their presence, in which case your mail center will upload your required documents for approval. We recommend that you contact your mail center prior to arriving to ensure this service is offered. If you live outside of the U.S. or have international documents: you are required to notarize online via proof.com . Please follow the instructions in your account and an email will be sent with a link to begin the online session. Your documents are automatically uploaded and submitted, including your Form 1583 and IDs. Note: Uploading documents from your account, email or fax submission is not allowed. If you need to add, edit or delete or update documents, please contact customer support and an agent will be able to assist. If you have U.S. documents and would like to visit your mail center to notarize, you must visit the location you signed up for. Other locations will not be able to notarize your documents. Local notaries, such as banks or the post office are not allowed. If you are an international customer or will be shipping internationally, you will be required to notarize online, using proof.com .

## What is the cost to notarize an additional person?

The cost to add another person to your notary session is $5.00 for each additional person that is notarized in the same session and are in the same room at the time of completing the session. This discount is provided only after reaching out to customer support to initiate the joint session. If the additional person is not in the same room at the time, the cost is $25.00. Note: Please contact customer support for assistance with setting up a joint session for multiple recipients. All individuals must be in the same room to complete the joint session at the discounted price. The joint session must be set up by customer support, please contact support to request this. If you are adding an additional person after you have completed your initial notary session, the price will be $25.00.

## Online Notary Requirements

The online notary is required when y ou do not have a Social Security Number or if you are shipping mail internationally. A desktop or mobile device: Video, microphone and audio are needed as well as a strong internet connection and access to your email. You will receive an email to initiate the online notary session. Fee: There is a $25 fee for a single notarization, a discount is provided to notarize multiple form 1583's if it is completed in the same session. Please contact customer support to set this up. Identification: 2 acceptable IDs from the list. 1 photo ID and 1 address ID (must match the name used to complete the form 1583). Acceptable Photo IDs: Valid state-issued driverâ€˜s license Non-driverâ€™s identification card U.S. Armed Forces card, Uniformed Service ID card U.S. permanent resident or other identification issued by U.S. Citizenship and Immigration Services U.S. passport, U.S. passport card Foreign passport Matricula Consular card (Mexico), NEXUS card (Canada) Acceptable Proof of Address Documents: Current lease Mortgage or deed of trust Voter or vehicle registration card Home or vehicle insurance policy Form I-94 Arrival and Departure record Unacceptable IDs: Social Security cards Credit cards Utility bills Birth certificates University ID Cards U.S. certificate of citizenship or naturalization Identification card issued by a federally or state-recognized tribal nation (tribal identification card) Note: The Primary ID must have a clear photograph of the mail recipient. International customers must use their passport as their photo ID. We accept the international equivalent of the Secondary IDs listed. Only the IDs listed here are accepted by iPostal1. If you have any questions or need clarification, please contact customer support.

## What will my address look like?

All our locations are approved by the USPS as a Commercial Mail Receiving Agency (CMRA). Most locations are professional retail pack and ship stores or business coworking centers in professional office buildings. Addresses vary by location and your personal mailbox number will most often appear on the same line as the street address. Some locations are suite addresses, the suite number will appear before your mailbox number. Note: It is important to use your full address, including your mailbox number and suite number if applicable, to ensure your mail arrives to the correct location. Sample address: Your Name or Company Name 123 Main Street #1001 Philadelphia, PA 123451

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Will I receive a mailbox number?

Upon signing up for your new virtual mailbox, you will automatically receive a unique mailbox number that is added to your new mailing address. It is important to include this mailbox number when addressing mail and updating your contacts. This will ensure that the correct mail is received to the correct mailbox. Note: The mailbox number is computer generated. You cannot choose your preferred mailbox number. Addresses vary by location. Some locations are suite addresses. Your personal mailbox number will most often appear on the same line as the street address. If your address contains a suite number, your mailbox will be next to the suite number. Sample address: Your Name or Company Name 123 Main Street #1001 Philadelphia, PA 123451

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Where does my mail go?

All mail and packages are received, stored and processed at the address you choose when you sign up. All our locations are approved by the USPS as a Commercial Mail Receiving Agency (CMRA). Most locations are professional retail pack and ship stores or business coworking centers in professional office buildings. Note: After your account is fully approved, you must inform your senders of your new address and/or file a Temporary Change of Address form with your local post office.

## Can I pickup my Mail?

Pickups are a service provided with all of our virtual mailbox plans at all locations. Your mail center is a physical location that will receive all mail and packages. You can choose to pick up mail at your mail center address during business hours, a small fee may be charged at the time of picking up. For the best service, we recommend scheduling a pickup before arriving to pick up mail, using the iPostal1 app. If applicable, the pickup fee will be collected at the time of pickup. To view your locations pick up fees: Go to iPostal1.com click on "Locations" on the top toolbar, s elect your location and click on "More Details" . Note: Pick up hours are different at each location. You can view your mail center hours in your account. If you may have any questions on pick up hours, please contact your mail center directly.

## Is there a minimum contract requirement?

We do not require contracts or lease agreements. You can sign up for an address and pay month to month with no sign up or cancellation fees. Save money and choose a yearly plan, paying for 10 months and getting 2 months free. Prepaid yearly plans are non-refundable after the first 30 days. Billing is automatically renewed unless you cancel your plan from your digital Mailbox or contact iPostal1 .

## Can I use this address to register my business, at a bank or to get a license or insurance?

The vast majority of states permit the use of a virtual mailing address to be used at the DMV, bank or to register a business, but the laws vary by state and change periodically, please check your local laws to determine what is permissible. Note: Images of your physical mail center location cannot be used as this only a virtual address subscription.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## How is an address with iPostal1 different from a PO Box?

iPostal1 mail center locations are real physical street addresses at professionally staffed, secure, and full-service mail centers or coworking space in professional buildings which can receive mail and packages from any carrier, including UPS and FedEx. All mail is easily managed virtually, y ou do not get an actual mailbox and key. PO Box: Only accepts USPS deliveries . You cannot use a PO box to register a business. You cannot manage your mail digitally with 24/7 access from anywhere. You have to physically check your mailbox with a PO box.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Will all my mail automatically be forwarded to my mailbox address?

The USPS will forward all first class mail if you file a "Change of Address" request with your local post office. Once your account is fully approved by your mail center, you can file a change of address. Please be sure it includes your full address, including your mailbox number. We recommend using the Temporary Change of Address form, good for 6 months and renewable, so that you can redirect forwarding if you need to change mailing address location in the future. A USPS Permanent Change of Address is not reversible in the future.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Can I send mail or packages to different addresses?

You are able to ship your mail items to the address listed on your form 1583. When filling out Form 1583, be sure to include the shipping address where you plan to send your items. After setting up your digital mailbox, you can easily request shipments and choose your preferred carrier and service level. Note: If you are planning to ship your mail internationally, you are required to use the online notary to notarize your documents.

## What is iWorkSpaceMail?

Our white label product allows you to offer the benefits of digital mailbox service to your current virtual and office members as an optional service or bundled as part of a service package. You set the pricing and invoice your members directly for the monthly mailbox fee and any additional services requested such as scanning or mail forwarding. You pay a small, fixed monthly fee per user, and the cost of any shipping labels used for mail forwarding. Benefits to your workspace: More revenue for longer - Members will pay for the convenience of this service and wonâ€™t want to give it up. A stronger brand - Position your brand as customer focused, innovative, and forward thinking. Happier members - No more missed important documents or waiting for mail to be forwarded. More efficient operations - Say goodbye to calls asking â€˜whatâ€™s in my boxâ€™ that waste staff time. Mail security and accessibility - A documented, organized process for managing mail and packages. How it works: Members use the app or website to view the outside of their mail items They request to forward, scan mail content, shred, or pick up. Manage your digital mailbox members and iPostal1 customers from the same login. There is no new technology for your team to learn. Integration: Coworking operators using DeskWorks or OfficeRnD will save time and effort with integrated billing. iWorkSpaceMail uses Syncaroo technology to automatically sync members, mailboxes and charges into your management systems. Once connected, monthly digital mailbox plans and tasks flow easily to the memberâ€™s monthly invoice produced by their operating platform. No need for separate tracking or reentering information. New members (with relevant plans or addons) will be synced to iWorkSpaceMail, and have digital mailboxes created automatically. Departing customers can also have their digital mailboxes disabled should they no longer have a plan that includes continued mailbox services. Through iWorkSpaceMail partnership with Syncaroo, keeping iWorkSpaceMail and your management system in sync is completely free. Of course there are still iWorkSpaceMail fees, but no paid Syncaroo account is necessary to keep things in sync.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## How does iWorkSpaceMail differ from iPostal1?

With iPostal1 we do all the marketing and sourcing of customers through our website and send them to you. We handle the 1583 process, billing, chargebacks, and customer service. With iWorkSpaceMail you sign up your own members and have access to our software to process mail on their behalf. You handle all aspects of customer service and billing and set your own pricing.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Whose responsibility is it to handle the 1583 process?

With iWorkSpaceMail you are signing up your own members, therefore, it is up to you to retrieve the required identifications and Form 1583 documentation and maintain the members documents in the USPS database. It is essential to establish a clear process for gathering, storing, and verifying IDs and Form 1583 documentation for every member you signup.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## How do I add an additional member to the iWorkSpaceMail platform?

Follow these steps to add an additional client to the iWorkSpaceMail platform: Log into the USZoom Admin Portal using your credentials. 1. Select " Manually Add Recipient" in the Recipient Admin tile. 2. C hoose the radial button have your location bill the recipient. Select "Virtual", then select a virtual plan from the dropdown menu. Check the box that you have the recipient's documents at your location. 3. Enter your member's personal information in the Fill in Recipient Data section. You can add a business name in the additional name field, however, accounts must be created under an individual. 4. Click "Add Recipient" . Your member will be assigned a mailbox number and sent an email with their login credentials and mailbox address information. Note: Your member will receive a welcome email, providing them with links to download the iWorkSpaceMail App to their Mobile Devices.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Will my members use the same app as the iPostal1 members?

No, your members will be instructed to download the iWorkSpaceMail App to access their digital mailbox account. This information is included in the login credential email they will receive when you add them to the platform. Note: The iWorkSpaceMail App will show your logo and will not show any task pricing with the exception of real time shipping prices.

## What if I need to remove an iWorkSpaceMail member from the system?

Follow the steps below to inactivate an iWorkSpaceMail member: 1. Click on "Recipient Lookup" under the Recipient Admin tile . 2. Search for the member by name or mailbox number, click Search . Then click on the search results. 3. Click on "Recipient Profile" , under the Recipients Details page. 4. Click on "Click here to inactivate this recipient", click "Ok" to confirm your selection. The member will be removed from the system.

## Do you provide iWorkSpaceMail customer service?

You are responsible for handling all aspects of customer service for your members.

## How much should I charge my iWorkSpaceMail members for the digital mailbox service?

You can choose to make this a standardized service as part of your membership packages or you can offer it as an additional optional service. Once you determine that, it is up to you to decide how much you would like to charge your members. We recommend a flat rate for mailbox services with the exception of mail forwarding which should be based on the shipping label cost.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Will my members see pricing?

We do not show pricing to your iWorkSpaceMail members with the exception of mail forwarding. You are free to charge your members whatever you decide within your membership agreement. The shipping rates we show your members are based on your established margins, carrier chosen, weight and dimensions of the item being shipped, and the shipping product chosen by the user.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Can I use iPostal1 shipping labels for my iWorkSpaceMail members?

Yes you can. When your members request to forward their mail, they will see pricing and carrier options. When you process the task, you will be given the option to choose an iPostal1 label or your own shipping label. If you choose to use the iPosatl1 label, the cost of the label will be posted to your next invoice.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Do my members need to schedule pickups using their iWorkSpaceMail app?

We recommend having your members schedule their pickups using the app which allows you to process and easily mark mail items as picked up within the system. It ensures the chain of custody of mail is complete and helps you track which items you are still responsible for as the CMRA.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## How will I get paid?

Since you do the billing and collection of payments for your iWorkSpaceMail members, we do not send you a commission. You will be invoiced based on the number of members active in our system and any shipping labels that have been used for the prior month. The invoice is generated and charged to your credit card on file the 1st of each calendar month.

We are available to assist you Monday to Friday 9:00 AM to 8:00 PM EST.

Enter your Username/Email address and then "Click" the " Submit" Button. Step 4. You will receive an email with a link that will allow you to enter a new password. Note: If you are having trouble resetting your password, please contact iPostal1 Customer Support.

## Can we have multiple Logins for each user?

Only one login is allowed per account. In order for other recipients to login to the iPostal1 account, you must share your login credentials for the account.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Can I receive mail for more than one business name?

The USPS only allows one business name per mailbox account. If you signed up for a business account you are allowed up to 1 business name. If you would like to receive mail for an additional business, you will be required to open a separate account for each additional business name, including an LLC or DBA.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Can I use the same 1583 Form for Multiple Locations?

To comply with USPS regulations, you must file a new 1583 form for each mailbox location you open. A discount is available when using the online notary service for multiple locations.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Do I need to create a new login for a second mailbox?

You can use the same login to access all mailboxes at all locations. Simply add the new mailbox within your account. If you may need assistance with merging accounts, please contact customer support directly.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Is mail automatically forwarded to my new address?

Mail and packages are not automatically forwarded to your new mailing address. Your virtual mailing address will only be available to the contacts and senders that you update. For mailbox locations in the U.S.: If you would like all mail to be forwarded to your new mailing address, y ou will need to fill out a separate USPS form to temporarily forward your mail. Once your account is fully approved by your mail center, we recommend visiting your local post office to fill out the form. For mailbox locations outside of the U.S.: Please contact your local post office for more information on how to forward your mail. Alternate option: Is to simply tell your contacts directly that your address has changed. This is what most customers do that want most of their mail still coming to their home address, and want the iPostal1 address to be there for business use. To ensure you receive mail to your new mailing address, after your account is fully approved: 1. Inform your senders and contacts of your new address. 2. File a Temporary Change of Address form with your local post office. Note: USPS will forward all First Class mail to your new address for 6 months at no charge and can be renewed for another 6 months. We do not recommend filing a Permanent Change of Address form with the USPS. If you file a Permanent Change of Address Form, the USPS will not forward mail from your iPostal1 mailing address to a new address later on. Any permanent address change can't be reverted if you would ever need to move your mail from iPostal1 to another place. For mailbox locations outside of the U.S. please contact your local post office for more information.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Can I use this address to register my business, at a bank or to get a driver's license, or get insurance?

Many customers have used our virtual mail address to register their businesses, at a bank or for the Department of Motor Vehicles/DMV. The vast majority of states permit the use of virtual mailing address, but the laws may vary by state and can change periodically. Please check the local laws to determine what's permissible.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Can I change my iPostal1 address?

You will be able to request for your account to be transferred to another mail center location. Please note when you change your address, you we will need to provide an updated notarized USPS Form 1583. Additional fees may apply when switching to a new location.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Where does my mail go if I cancel my account?

If you have filed a "Temporary Change of Address form" with your post office, you can easily cancel the temporary address change and file a new one. To correct or modify a change of address order, you can use the "USPS Form 3546". I f you have filed a Permanent Change of Address form, you will need to inform your senders individually that your address has changed. Note: If no forwarding option is filed, any new mail that is received at your mail center will be returned to sender.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Can I still have mail come to my house if I have an iPostal1 Virtual Address?

Your mail can still come to your house. Many customers use the iPostal1 address as an additional address. If you do not fill out a Change of Address form with USPS, your mail coming to your home will not be affected.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Is my location a registered agent?

Some mail center address locations are registered agents. This is not a service provided directly by iPostal1. Please contact your location directly for more information on registered agent service and for additional pricing information. You can view if your address provides registered agent service when looking up your address on iPostal1.com: Click on "Locations" located at the top of the page. Select your location. Click on " More Details ".

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Can you provide a proof of address letter, lease or contract?

We do not provide a lease agreement or contracts for a virtual mailbox. If you may need a rental agreement or proof of address letter, we recommend using your iPostal1 invoice as valid documentation. The iPostal1 invoice contains your name, billing address, and account information. Many institutions accept such documents as a valid proof of address if they are recent and clearly show your name and the address in question. &#128269; How to locate your invoice: 1. Log in to your account on a mobile browser or desktop, c lick the dropdown menu next to your username in the Top Menu Bar. 2. Click "Transactions", locate your invoice and click "View Details" on the far-right side of your screen. You can filter the date range to view all transactions. 3. The invoice will open with the option to print as proof of address. Note: You can also use the welcome email you received from iPostal1 after your account approval. This email contains your full U.S. mailbox address, including the suite number, and is considered a valid proof of address. This email can be located in your inbox. If you still need further proof, such as a letter, please contact customer support directly for assistance.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Can I have mail or a package delivered at another location?

If you are traveling and need to have mail delivered to another address, you will be required to add a new location and submit the required documents for each location. Note: When signing in to your account, you can easily toggle between mail center locations and manage your mail items.

## How does Virtual Office Plan work?

When you select a virtual office plan, you will be prompted to choose a local or toll-free phone and fax number after you log in to your personal Digital Mailbox. You can receive incoming calls to this virtual number and the call will automatically be forwarded to the phone number of your choice. You can receive and review fax conveniently from within your account. Your forwarding number can easily be changed at any time. You'll have an option to customize how many times the phone will ring before being forwarded to your voicemail. You can set your own voice message or type in the wording for a professional automated message. You'll receive a notification when a voicemail is received. You can easily listen to your voice messages from the iPostal1 app or your iPostal1 online mailbox. Outgoing fax is not a supported feature at this time. When you receive a call to your virtual phone number, the Caller ID will display your virtual phone number. This helps you to easily recognize these calls. We suggest saving your virtual phone number as a contact to allow you to quickly identify the source of the call.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## What is included in a Virtual Office plan and how does it work

When choosing a virtual office plan, you will receive a mailing address for your business, along with all the features of our Digital Mailbox service. What makes our Virtual Office plans different, is that you also get a phone line with call forwarding and voicemail capabilities, so you can have a business number linked to your mailing address and avoid using your personal phone for business. If you sign up for our Virtual Office plan, you receive: Virtual mailing address. Phone forwarding. Voice mail messaging with personal greeting. A dedicated electronic fax placed into your digital mailbox as a PDF. Note: Phone forwarding at iPostal1 addresses outside the U.S s available on a limited basis.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## What is the price for phone and fax services?

Virtual Office plans start at $39.99 per month. This includes a real physical street address, complete Digital Mailbox service, phone forwarding, voice mail messaging, and fax line. Competitive rates per call and per fax apply.

If you do not have a Virtual Office plan, you can change your plan by clicking mailbox settings in the sidebar, and selecting "Change Plan" under General Settings.

## Do I have a virtual phone and fax number?

A virtual phone and fax line is provided when you sign up for a Virtual Office plan. These numbers can be set up directly from your digital mailbox. You can choose your phone number and add additional phone and fax lines by clicking "Phone and Fax Settings" in the sidebar. Note: This feature will allow you to receive and review voicemails and will allow you to receive and review fax, all within your account inbox. Outgoing fax is not a supported feature at this time.

## Can I receive a traditional fax to my location?

You can receive a traditional fax, if the service is available at your mail center location. Your fax will display in your mailbox, just as a mail item. When sending a fax, your name and mailbox number should appear clearly on the fax cover sheet to ensure it is uploaded to mailbox correctly. You can find your locations fax number in the "Contact Us" page, when logged into your dashboard. Pricing to receive a fax: $2.00 each fax, up to 6 pages. $0.25 each additional page.

## Can I receive a fax with my virtual office plan?

Our virtual office plan, offers a fax number in which you can receive and review all fax that are received but i f you do not have a virtual office plan and would like to receive a fax, y ou can receive a traditional fax to your mail center, only if the service is available at your mail center location. If traditional fax service is provided at your location, y ou can find your location's fax number in the "Contact Us" page, when logged into your dashboard. Your fax will display in your inbox, just as a mail item. When sending a fax to your location, your name and mailbox number should appear clearly on the fax cover sheet to ensure it is uploaded to your mailbox correctly. Note: You can always choose to upgrade to a virtual plan at any time by clicking mailbox settings in the sidebar, and selecting "Change Plan" under "General Settings".

## Can I call out from my Virtual Office phone line?

Your Virtual Office Phone line can take incoming calls and messages only and cannot be used to make outgoing phone calls.
