## How much mail can I receive every month?

Your selected plan level determines how much mail you can receive each month. This includes all types of mail items from letters to packages. Monthly Limit per Plan: Green Plan - 30 mail items per month. Blue Plan - 60 mail items per month. Silver Plan - 120 mail items per month. Gold Plan - 240 mail items per month. Note: An additional fee of $.35 per mail item, will be applied for e a ch additional mail item that exceeds your monthly plan limit. You can always upgrade your plan at any time, if needed.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Can I Receive Large Packages?

You can receive large packages but if you plan on receiving mail larger than 100 lbs, it is helpful to contact your mail center location to make sure they will be able to accommodate a package of that size. Note: Your mail centers contact information can be found in your account after your account is fully approved.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Can I receive mail addressed to other people?

The United States Postal Service requires a notarized USPS form 1583 and 2 acceptable forms of identification for any person or additional name that will be receiving mail to your account. Please reach out for assistance with adding an additional recipient. Additional recipients are required to notarize the form 1583 via proof.com's video notary session. Note: Personal accounts are allowed up to 6 recipients in total, including the account holder. Business accounts are allowed up to 1 business name and 6 recipient names in total, including the account holder. Locations in Canada are limited to 1 customer name per account

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Can I Change my Plan?

You may change your monthly plan at any time directly from your account. Any changes made will be effective the next billing period. However, you may not change from a yearly plan to a monthly plan until the yearly billing period ends. Monthly plans can be upgraded to any other plan, including a yearly plan. Yearly plans can be upgraded to another yearly plan that allows for more mail items per month.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Are scans included in my subscription plan?

The images of the outside of your mail items are viewable in your inbox and is included free of charge, up to the monthly limit of the plan that you choose. You may request a scan of the inside contents for any mail item for a small additional fee. Scanning bundles are available at discounted prices. For as low as $9.99 per month, you get all the benefits of viewing and managing your mail with an app from wherever you find yourself. This is a great value (more convenience and more features for a lot less than renting a PO Box). We keep your monthly cost low by charging for additional services only when you request them, this way you only pay for what you use. Note: For full details on iPostal1 services and pricing, see our "Pricing" pages. You will find services with fees listed under 'Optional Services'.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Is forwarding mail included in the subscription and how much will it cost?

The cost of forwarding is not included in any subscription plan. Each mail item that you request to ship, will be charged separately. The price is determined by the mail item type, weight/ dimensions, carrier and shipping speed. Prices are set by your mail center. iPostal1 shows real-time shipping prices for any shipment you make by carrier (UPS, FedEx, USPS) and by level of service (overnight, 2-day, ground, etc.), and you choose the shipping that best meets your budget and timing needs. Note: You can choose to consolidate all mail items into one package to save on shipping.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You will be prompted to enter your business name and pay the difference in price for the plan selected. Note: Only one business name is allowed per mailbox number. If you have multiple business names, a separate mailbox plan will be required for each business name. To upgrade to a business plan: 1. Log in to your iPostal1 account on a desktop or mobile browser. 2. Click on " Mailbox Settings" located in the left toolbar. 3. Click the "Change Plan" button under general settings. 4. Scroll down to see all your options and select the business plan that suits your needs. 5. Review your plan and click "Place Order". Your primary credit card will be charged for the new subscription rate. You will be prompted to enter your business name.

## How to navigate the Inbox tab

The Inbox tab can be found on the left toolbar and shows you all of your mail and the outside image(s) of each mail item. Step 1. To sort your mail items in your inbox click the " Show" drop-down box to view Open Requests, Scanned Items, Letters & Large Envelopes, Packages & Letter Packs, or Stored Items. Step 2. You can also sort your mail items by the date received. Click on the " Sort By" drop-down box to choose the earliest or the latest items received. Step 3. To make a request for your mail to be processed, select your mail items and choose from the menu options in the t op toolbar.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Do you automatically open and scan my mail?

Mail is kept secure and confidential, w hen items arrive you will be notified via email or push notifications via our free iPostal1 App. We open your mail only if you specifically request us to scan the contents. The price of scanning a letter starts at $2.25 per letter, up to 10 pages. We open packages only when you request us to take a picture of package content, or in order to ensure compliance with shipping regulations. Note: You can choose the auto-scan feature in which all letters that are received to your account are automatically requested for a content scan. This additional feature is only for letters and does not include boxes and packages.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Can Someone else pick up my mail?

Anyone handling mail in your account is required to be listed on the account as a recipient. If your mailbox location is in the U.S. the additional recipient must submit a notarized Form 1583 and two forms of ID. Please contact customer support for assistance with adding an additional person to your account for pick up. We recommend informing your mail center of an alternate person collecting your mail and confirming their guidelines for this arrangement.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Can I use my iPostal1 Mailing Address to receive Google Pin Codes?

While some customers have successfully registered with companies like Google and D&B, we cannot guarantee that all our addresses will comply with their address requirements for these companies. We suggest reviewing Googleâ€™s requirements for participating in their Google My Business program. Note: Not all iPostal1 locations accept the Google My Business program pin. You are welcomed to sign up and if you choose to cancel your account within 30 days of signing up, we can process a refund request, as long as your account has not been used to receive mail or for any other reasons.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## What should I do about junk mail

Most mail center locations will carefully sort out and recycle or discard all junk mail, such as flyers, circulars, advertising, and catalogs that are classified by the USPS as Standard Mail. When junk mail is discarded before hand, it does not count toward your items per month received. If you receive any unsolicited junk mail that is uploaded to your account, you may choose to discard it at no additional charge. Discarding mail that is already inserted is an included feature at no extra cost. Note: You can choose to subscribe to our App based service to stop junk mail at an additional fee of $9.99 for 3 months. To find more information or to sign up for iStopMail, login to your account and locate iStopMail on the left toolbar.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## When can I begin receiving mail

To begin receiving mail to your mail center address, your account and documents must be fully approved by your mail center location. Please submit your notarized form 1583 and 2 acceptable IDs. I f your account is not yet approved, mail items will be returned to the sender according to USPS regulations.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## How are shipping requests handled

Shipments are sent based on the carrier and timeline that you choose and your destination address. Many mail centers offer all levels of shipping services from USPS, FedEx and UPS. You will only receive a tracking number, if you select a trackable shipping method. Your tracking number will usually include a delivery date. Note: Tracking is not included for USPS standard/single letters and USPS First Class Mail. If you are shipping time sensitive or important mail, we recommend choosing a trackable shipping method.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Are there any items that I cannot ship?

Please see the USPS Do Not Ship List for domestic shipment and export restrictions from and within the U.S. Hazardous materials that may not be shipped include perfume, alcohol, hair spray, spray paint, and any other flammable or pressurized items. All packages exported from the U.S. must comply with the iPostal1 Export Policy .

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Who is listed as the sender of a forwarded package?

Any mail item that is shipped from your mail center, will include your locations return address, your mailbox number and the name associated with your account, including your business name if applicable.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## What is a Mail Item?

A mail item is anything that arrives in your iPostal1 mailbox: any letter, package, or large envelope is one mail item.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Do you open my Mail?

All iPostal1 addresses are approved by the USPS as a Commercial Mail Receiving Agency (CMRA). All your mail is kept secure and confidential, your mail center will only open your mail when you specifically request a scan, box image or a shipping task. Your mail center will open your mail: If you request a scan- your mail center will open the letter and scan the inside contents. If you request a box image- your mail center will open your package and take images of the inside contents. If you request to ship a package- your mail center may open your package in order to ensure compliance with shipping regulations.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Can I send mail in my business name instead of my personal name.

If you have selected a business plan, you can choose to receive mail in your business name instead of your personal name. If you do not have a business plan and you receive mail under a business name, your mail will be returned to sender.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Note: You can add an additional location directly on your account, by selecting â€˜Add new Mailboxâ€™ and select your prefered subscription plan. You will be required to provide a new notarized form 1583 and a 2 acceptable IDs for the new address. The new account will be merged to your existing account and will share the same login information, as well as a payment method.

## Plan pricing

Your monthly plan varies by the plan and location you selected. All plans includes a specific amount of mail items to receive per month. You will notice separate prices for business plans, if you included a business name to your account. Pricing may vary based on your mail center location. The majority of our locations are Standard locations and start at the $9.99 price. Standard , Select , Premium , or Prestige locations each have different starting prices. Starting price for Virtual Mailing Address Plans ( Standard location) Green - $9.99 per month (30 mail items per month) Blue - $14.99 per month (60 mail items per month) Silver - $24.99 per month (120 mail items per month) Gold - $39.99 per month (240 mail items per month) Starting price for Virtual Business Address Plans ( Standard location) Business Green - $14.99 per month (30 mail items per month) Business Blue - $19.99 per month (60 mail items per month) Business Silver - $29.99 per month (120 mail items per month) Business Gold - $44.99 per month (240 mail items per month) Note: You may notice tax is charged for your mailbox account, if your mail center is in Canada or located in a state that charges tax for mailbox services.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## How are yearly/annual plans charged?

Yearly plans renew only once a year. When you subscribe annually, youâ€™ll pay for ten months and receive two months free. This discount is included in the total price you pay. Example: Yearly Green Plan 30 = $99 per year. Monthly Green Plan 30 starts at $9.99 per month = $119.88 per year. Note: Our $99 annual subscription plan saves you two months on subscription fees. Billing is automatically renewed unless you cancel your plan before the renewal date. Prepaid yearly plans are non-refundable after the first 30 days.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Why is the Mailbox Monthly Fee not the same at all locations?

Roughly 90% of our locations are Standard addresses with monthly subscription plans starting at $9.99/month. However, addresses in prestigious buildings or in locations where costs and demand are higher, may cost more according to the address type. Starting prices based addre ss type: Select Address: +$10 Premium Address: +$20 Prestige Address: +$30

## Why do I need a credit card and what if I don't have one?

We require a valid payment method or an active credit card to be listed on your account in order to keep your account active. We will charge you each calendar month or year based on the plan you selected and the date you signed up. Any applicable taxes will also be included in that amount. Without a credit card or valid payment method on file, your account will not be activated for use.

## How do I pay my Subscription and when is it due?

Your subscription payment is automatically billed using the primary credit card on file. You are billed each month or year, on the same day you signed up and depending on the plan you selected. To view and change the card on file: Click on the drop down located on the top right, next to your username. Click on "Account Setting s". click " Payment Method" . ## My credit card is not going through, what should I do?

Our system will automatically process your credit card in real-time. Please follow these steps if you are having trouble updating your payment method. If your credit card is not being accepted by the system- Please enter a different credit card. If your payment is being denied or declined - Please contact your bank or financial institution. If you would like to change your payment method - You can choose to use PayPal as your payment method, if your mailbox number is located in Canada, PayPal will not be available to choose. If you continue to experience an issue- Please update the iPostal1 app or sign in to your account on a desktop or mobile browser.

## How to update your Payment Method

To change your payment method from PayPal to credit card or credit card to PayPal: Step 1. Log in to your account on a desktop or mobile browser. Click on the drop down arrow, located at the top right, next to your username. Click "Account Settings" . Step 2. Click " Payment Method", located on the right side of your screen, under " Account Features" . Step 3. Select your desired payment type (Credit Card or PayPal) and follow the steps to add the updated information. (PayPal is not applicable for Canadian locations) Note: If your mailbox is located in Canada, you will not be able to choose PayPal as a payment method.

## Do I have to pay to pick up my Mail?

Since digital mailboxes are not self-service like physical mailboxes, some mail centers charge a nominal fee for processing and retrieving your mail when you come in to pick it up. Pick up fees may charged, depending on the mail item type and depending on your mail center. Note: To view your locations pick up fees on iPostal1.com , click on "Locations" on the top toolbar, s elect your location and click on "More Details".

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## PayPal Payment Overview

Paying with PayPal is a convenient and secure way to make payments for your online mailbox. Your Paypal information will be requested during checkout. When paying with PayPal, y ou will be required to maintain a minimum balance above $20.00 on your account. When the account drops below the minimum of $20.00 , you are automatically charged to maintain a balance for the account minimum. T his ensures that your subscription and account will remain active. Not e: You will be prompted to agree to the Paypal Terms of Agreement before signing up. Your first payment will include the subscription fee and $25 toward your Paypal balance . Any unused PayPal funds is refundable, if you choose to close your account in the future. Recharge options: $20, $25, $50 and $100.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## PayPal Minimum Balance

Your Paypal Account requires a minimum $20 balance. When your account falls below $20, your account will renew for $20. The PayPal Terms of Agreement before sign up requires all customers to agree to the minimum balance requirement.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## PayPal Payments for Canada Mailboxes

We will no longer accept PayPal as a payment method for iPostal1 digital mailboxes located in Canada. If you mailbox is located in Canada please enter a credit card as your payment method.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## If I cancel my account, when will I be refunded for my PayPal Balance?

If you choose to cancel your iPostal1 Mailbox account, the remainder of the PayPal balance will be returned to your PayPal account with 5-7 business days.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Where can I find pricing for additional services?

To view services provided with your plan: 1. On the iPostal1 website, click on "Pricing" located at the top of the page. 2. Choose your plan: Virtual Mailing address, Virtual Business Address or Virtual Office. 3. Scroll down to view all included services and optional services provided with your plan.

## What is included in my plan?

Your inbox has many features that are automatically included at no additional cost: Real physical street address. Flexible shipment scheduling. (on request, weekly, bi-weekly, monthly) Personal Digital Mailbox - access online or with an app to manage mail. Your choice of carriers, ship dates, speed and service level. Free App for Android and iPhone. 24/7 digital access to all your mail items, unlimited secure cloud storage for scans and voice messages. 30 day storage: all mail & letterpacks; packages under 1,728 cu inches (= 12x12x12 size package) See a picture of the outside of every mail item. 10 day free storage: packages 1,728 to 4,895 cu inches. Sender information for every item clearly visible. 5 day free storage: packages at/over 4,896 cu inches (= 24x17x12 size package) Automatic email alert for new items received. Discard or dipose mail items. Preparation of commercial invoice. (for international shipments) Consolidation of letters into one package for forwarding. Virtual Mailing Address plans include up to 6 recipient names per address. To view all services provided with your plan click here or follow the steps below: 1. On the iPostal1 website, click on "Pricing" , located at the top of the page. 2. Choose your plan: Virtual Mailing address, Virtual Business Address or Virtual Office. 3. Scroll down to view all included services and optional service provided with your plan.

## Pickup price

When picking up mail from your mail center, you may be charged a small fee for picking up your mail. Each location has its own pickup pricing that is viewable on our website. You can view your locations pickup prices on our locations page. Prices range from $0 - $7.00 depending on the mail item type, size and quantity. Letters and post cards : are charged all together as one fee for any amount of letters, when picked up all at once in the same visit. Package s: are charged per package, depending on the size. Note: Pickup fees are due at the time of picking up your mail and it is charged to the payment method on file for your account. Some locations may offer free pick ups, please visit the locations page to view each mail centers individual fees. To view your locations pickup pricing: Step 1. Go to iPostal1.com . Step 2. Click on " Locations" , located on the top toolbar. Step 3. Locate your mailing address. Step 4. Click " Click for More Details" , just below to show the exact pickup price for your mail center.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Shipping and Consolidation

We offer comprehensive shipping services from all major carriers: USPS, FedEx and UPS. When you login to your account and choose to ship your mail, you will be able to select from the levels of service and pricing that fits your needs. Shipping carrier and international shipping may vary by location. Shipping Prices: Our system will provide an estimated shipping quote based on your mail center, the carrier, speed of shipping and dimensional weight. A dditional fees may be applied to the quote/ regular shipping charges such as for labor and packaging materials. Consolidation Prices: No charge for any number of letters consolidated. $1.95 per package or letter-pack consolidated. $1.95 for any number of magazines consolidated. Additional charge for packaging materials may be applied. Prepaid labels are not accepted. Note: If you are shipping multiple items of various sizes together, we recommend you use the Consolidate feature, which will provide you a quote before shipping your mail items. When choosing "Consolidate and Ship", you will not see an estimated price until after your mail center weighs all of the mail items and processes the request. To view a quoted price, we recommend choosing a consolidation of mail first. When updating a shipping address, please ensure that all shipping addresses that are entered, are valid, verified and recognized by USPS to avoid any delivery issues. Storage fees will continue to be charged per mail item until the mail item is shipped.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Check Deposit

Check deposit is a great feature that can be used to conveniently deposit checks from your iPostal1 Mailbox directly to your bank account via mail. Each check that you would like deposited will need to be scanned first, before you can proceed to request a check deposit task. You can view if your mail center location offers check deposit on the iPostal1 website, click on "Locations" at the top of the page, select your location and click "More Details". Note: The cost for each check deposit request is $4.95, plus the cost of trackable USPS Shipping (on average $11-15) You may deposit up to 5 checks per check deposit request. You can track your check deposit shipment with the tracking number provided. This service is available in most locations but limited to Mail Centers in the United States. Please contact your mail center directly to see if this service is provided.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Scanning, Shredding and Bundle prices

Photos of the outside of your mail items are included with your plan. If you would like to view the inside contents of your mail item, you must request a scan for each item. An additional fee is charged per scan request. Discarding of mail item is usually free of charge, if you would like to shred the mail item instead, a fee is charged for each shredding request. The fee for a single scan or shred request is $2.25 per letter, up to 10 pages, and an additional $0.25 per additional page. To save money on the cost of scanning the inside contents of your mail or shredding your mail, you can purchase a bundle. Scan and shred bundles can be purchased directly through your account and are more economical. With these prepaid bundles, you can use them as needed. Bundle Prices per envelope: $10.00 for 5 scans or shred orders. Save 10%* $18.00 for 10 scans or shred orders. Save 20%* $30.00 for 20 scans or shred orders. Save 33%* *up to 10 pages per order Order size = 1 envelope Note: Bundles are non-refundable but can be applied to multiple addresses on merged accounts, and they do not expire.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Image of invoice and package contents

You can request the image of a package to view the inside contents or to view the invoice. Your mail center will open your package and take pictures of the inside contents and invoice. Each request includes up to 6 images of 1 mail item. Image of invoice and/or package contents - Image of invoice only: $2.95 Image of contents only: $3.95 Image of both invoice and contents: $5.95

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Receive Fax

You can recieve a traditional fax at your mail center location, if your mail center provides this service. Once the fax is received it will it will be viewable within your account just as a regular mail item. When sending a fax, your name and mailbox number should appear clearly on the fax cover sheet to ensure it is uploaded to mailbox correctly. Note: Please contact your mail center to see if they provide this service. If your location provides fax service, you can find your locations fax number in the "Contact Us" page, when logged into your dashboard. Pricing to receive a traditional fax: $2.00 each fax, up to 6 pages. $0.25 each additional page.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Receive additional mail items over my monthly limit

If you receive additional mail items outside of your plan limit per month, you will be charged a small fee for each extra mail item that is received. Pricing for Mail items above plan maximum: $0.35 per item Note: If you are planning to receive a high amount of mail, over the plan limit please contact customer support to discuss your options.

## iStopMail

iStopMail is a mobile based subscription App that prevents physical junk mail from being sent to your mail center, home or workplace. Simply take a photo of your unwanted mail and click â€œUnsubscribeâ€ to remove yourself from one of our partnerâ€™s marketing lists. In just 24 hours, youâ€™ll receive a notification confirming you have been successfully unsubscribed. The app is always available to monitor the progress of your requests. Our close collaboration with source companies allows us to assist with unsubscribing you from catalogs, magazines, credit card offers, and more. Note: This service is only for physical mail and not email. For more information on your i Stop Mail plan, please contact customer support. iStopMail prices: $9.99 for 3 months plan.

## Notarize Any Document

This feature allows you to notarize any document, aside from your iPostal1 form 1583. You will have access to an online notary and have your documents notarized under 15 minutes. Note: This service cannot be used during the signup up process, to notarized your iPostal1 documents for account approval. Notarize Any Documents price: $25.00 per session. Additional fees are charged for multiple pages. Additional fees are charged per additional signers.

## Personal Delivery

Personal Delivery allows you to schedule the delivery of your mail items directly to your home. You can pick a date and time that works for you and a driver will deliver your mail.

## Business Compliance BOI

The U.S. Department of Treasury's Financial Crimes Enforcement Network (FinCEN) requires many American businesses to file a "Beneficial Ownership Information" (BOI) Report. As part of a new suite of business-oriented features, iPostal1 has partnered with a third party agency to offer a special rate for BOI filing assistance. It has no bearing on your mail center nor does it require any action on your part. You should consult with your legal and financial advisors to determine if the mandate applies to your business before deciding if they want to take advantage of this optional add-on service. If you are attempting to submit your business compliance forms for the first time or should you require further assistance with the BOI form, please contact the BOI directly. If you already began the process and you need assistance, please use the chat icon on the bottom right corner of the BOI page in your dashboard. This will connect you to the third party vendor. Note: Business Compliance forms are not required for an iPostal1 account appr

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Extended storage for mail items

You receive 30 days free storage for all letters, magazines, letter packs. Packages are given 5 - 10 days, depending on the size. Once your expiration date is expired, you will begin to be charged storage. Letters and flat mail are charged $1.10/item per month. Packages that exceed 1,728 cubic inches (equivalent to 12" x 12" x 12") are given 10 days free storage. Packages that exceed 4,895 cubic inches (equivalent to 24" x 17" x 12") are given 5 days free storage. Note: Packages are charged $1.10/pound* per every 5, 10, or 30 days - According to the size and storage time frame allotted to the package. * Greater of actual weight or dimensional weight. To avoid storage charges, recycle, shred, forward, or pick up mail items within your free storage period. Once the free storage period has exceeded, all storage fees will be applied automatically. You do not have to do anything extra in your account.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## How to request a refund?

If you qualify and would like to request a refund, please contact customer support directly and an agent will be happy to assist you. All refunds must be approved before processing. Subscription: If your account has been cancelled within the first 30 days of sign up and has been unused, you may be eligible to request a refund of your subscription fee. Prepaid yearly plans are non-refundable after the first 30 days. All other refunds: Please contact customer support. Online Notary: Notary fees via proof.com are non refundable.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Can the rest of my annual subscription be refunded?

If you choose to close your account within the first 30 days of opening and your mailbox has not been used for any reason, you may be eligible for a refund of your . Prepaid yearly plans are non-refundable after the first 30 days. Billing is automatically renewed unless you cancel your plan before the renewal date.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## When will I receive my refund?

If you qualify for a refund for your subscription fees and you have already requested a refund with a customer support agent, it will generally take 3-5 business days to process. All other refunds will need to be approved before processing and can take longer at times.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## How to cancel my account using a desktop

You can cancel your account at any time by logging into your account on a mobile browser or desktop. Before canceling your mailbox , please empty your inbox by discarding, shipping, or shredding your mail items. Please ensure you have made copies of all uploaded documents, as they will be deleted when your account is canceled. If you would like to re-activate your account, your mailbox number will be saved for 90 days. Once your account is closed, mail will no longer be accepted at your location. Please remember to update your contacts with your new mailing address. If you are not able to click the cancel button, please verify that you have cleared all of the mail items in your inbox and are up to date with your payment. To cancel your account using a desktop browser: Step 1. Login to your account on a desktop or mobile browser. Click on "Mailbox Settings" , located in the left toolbar. Step 2. Scroll down to the bottom of the Mailbox Setting box and click the " Cancel Mailbox" button. Note: If you don't see this option, please take action on your mail items by selecting a discard, shipping or shred. After your mailbox is empty, come back to this page, and the Cancel Mailbox button will be active. Step 3. To finalize the cancellation of your iPostal1 Digital Mailbox, click " O k" . You will then receive an email confirmation that your account has been canceled. You will no longer be charged for your subscription.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## How to cancel my account in the iPostal1 App

You can choose to cancel your account at any time in the iPostal1 app: Once you Delete your location, your account will be cancelled and closed completely , mail will not be accepted at your location. If you would like to reopen your account, your mailbox number will be saved for 90 days. If 90 days have passed, please contact customer support for assistance. Please remember to update your contacts with your new mailing address. If the Cancel Mailbox link is not clickable, please be sure your payment is up to date. To cancel your account in the iPostal1 App: Step 1. Log into your account in the iPostal1 App, using your username or password. Step 2. Tap on the " Menu" button in the top left corner. Be sure that all mail is cleared from your inbox. Step 3. Tap on " Account Settings", below your mailbox address. Step 4. Tap " Delete Location" . Step 5. The system will ask you to confirm that this is what you would like to do. If you cancel your account by mistake, please contact customer support.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## How can I confirm that my account is closed?

When you close your account successfully, you will receive an automated email confirming the closure of your account. This email confirmation will be sent to the email you used to signup. If you closed your account accidently or if you did not receive this email, please contact customer support for assistance.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## How to reopen my account?

If you would like to reinstate your account, simply login, pay any outstanding balance. Your mailbox number will be saved for 90 days. If 90 days have passed, please contact customer support for assistance. Note: If you don't have an address linked, you can add your preferred address and select a plan. You will also be required to submit the required documents for account approval. Please contact support if you may need assistance.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Technical issues on the website

If you are experiencing issues with our website such as invalid token or server error : 1. Clear Browser Cache and Cookies : Sometimes, old cookies and cached data can cause issues with website functionality. 2. Use another browser : Using another browser such as google, chrome, safari, edge or incognito/private browsing mode can help bypass some browser-related issues. 3. Check Browser Settings : Ensure that your browser is set to accept cookies and that there are no extensions blocking the website's functionality. 4. Update Browser : Make sure your browser is up-to-date to avoid compatibility issues. 5. Contact Support : If the issue persists, it may be helpful to contact our support team for further assistance.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## Technical issues in the App

Although it is not common, but if youâ€™re experiencing issues with the iPostal1 app, such as invalid token, server error or not viewing all of your mail items, please follow the steps below: 1. Update App - Please ensure your app is updated to the latest version. 2. Reinstall App - If no updates are available, we recommend uninstalling and reinstalling the app, as this often resolves common technical issues. 3. Login on a desktop or mobile browser - If the issue persists, please login to the iPostal1 website, using your mobile browser or desktop computer to see any updates. Note: At times there may be a delay in viewing recently inserted mail items, we suggest signing in to the desktop version of your account as it will have the most up to date information. If your screen is greyed and not accessible, please verify if your account is fully approved/ active and your payment information is up to date. If you continue to have an issue, please contact customer support.
